<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Item 8.01. &nbsp;<U>Other Events</U>.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>The Registrant registered issuances of Mortgage Pass-Through Certificates, Series 2004-15F on a delayed or continuous basis pursuant to Rule 415 under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, by a Registration Statement on Form S-3 (Registration File No. 333-120274) (the &#147;Registration Statement&#148;). &nbsp;Pursuant to the Registration Statement, the Registrant issued $545,870,163.00 aggregate principal amount of the Class 1A-1, Class 1A-2, Class 1A-3, Class 1A-4, Class 2A-1, Class 2A-2, Class 2A-3, Class 2A-4, Class 3A-1, Class 3A-2, Class 4A-1, Class 5A-1, Class 6A-1, Class 7A-1, Class 7A-2, Class A-X, Class A-P, Class B1, Class B2 and Class B3 Certificates (the &#147;Publicly Offered Certificates&#148;) on December 17, 2004. &nbsp;This Current Report on Form 8-K is being filed to satisfy an undertaking, contained in the definitive Prospectus dated December 1, 2
004, as supplemented by the Prospectus Supplement dated December 14, 2004 and the supplement to the Prospectus Supplement dated December 17, 2004, to file a copy of the Master Servicing and Trust Agreement (as defined below) and other operative agreements executed in connection with the issuance of the Publicly Offered Certificates, a form of which was filed as an exhibit to the Registration Statement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>The Publicly Offered Certificates were issued pursuant to a Master Servicing and Trust Agreement (the &#147;Trust Agreement&#148;), attached hereto as <U>Exhibit 4.5.1</U>, dated as of November 1, 2004, among GS Mortgage Securities Corp., as depositor, Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, as master servicer, JPMorgan Chase Bank, National Association, as securities administrator and custodian, and Wachovia Bank, National Association, as Trustee, which incorporates by reference the Standard Terms to Master Servicing and Trust Agreement, November 2004 Edition (the &#147;Standard Terms&#148;), attached hereto as <U>Exhibit 4.5.2</U>. &nbsp;The &#147;Certificates&#148; consist of the Publicly Offered Certificates and the Class B4, Class B5, Class B6 and Class R Certificates. &nbsp;The Certificates evidence all of the beneficial ownership interest in a trust fund that consi
sts primarily of a pool of certain conventional, fixed rate, residential mortgage loans with an aggregate outstanding principal balance of approximately $548,613,754.22 as of December 1, 2004, together with certain other assets. &nbsp;Capitalized terms used herein and not otherwise defined shall have the meanings assigned to them in the Trust Agreement and the Standard Terms.</P>

<TITLE>EXHIBIT 4.5.1</TITLE>

<BODY style="line-height:12pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>

<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>GSR MORTGAGE LOAN TRUST 2004-15F</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>MORTGAGE PASS-THROUGH CERTIFICATES</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>MASTER SERVICING AND TRUST AGREEMENT</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><BR></P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767936"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">THIS MASTER SERVICING AND TRUST AGREEMENT (this &#147;<U>Trust Agreement</U>&#148;), dated as of November 1, 2004, is hereby executed by and among GS MORTGAGE SECURITIES CORP., a Delaware corporation (the &#147;<U>Depositor</U>&#148;), WACHOVIA BANK, NATIONAL ASSOCIATION, as trustee (the &#147;<U>Trustee</U>&#148;) under this Trust Agreement and the Standard Terms to Master Servicing and Trust Agreement, November 2004 Edition (the &#147;<U>Standard Terms</U>&#148;), JPMORGAN CHASE BANK, NATIONAL ASSOCIATION, as securities administrator (in such capacity, the &#147;<U>Securities Administrator</U>&#148;) and custodian (in such capacity, the &#147;<U>Custodian</U>&#148;), and CHASE MANHATTAN MORTGAGE CORPORATION, as master servicer (the &#147;<U>Master Servicer</U>&#148;), all of the provisions of which, unless otherwise specified herein, are incorporated her
ein and shall be a part of this Trust Agreement as if set forth herein in full.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>PRELIMINARY STATEMENT</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Board of Directors of the Depositor has duly authorized the formation of GSR Mortgage Loan Trust 2004-15F as a trust (the &#147;<U>Trust</U>&#148;) to issue a series of securities with an aggregate initial outstanding principal balance of $548,613,753.82 to be known as the Mortgage Pass-Through Certificates, Series 2004-15F (the &#147;<U>Certificates</U>&#148;). &nbsp;The Trust is formed by this Trust Agreement. &nbsp;The Certificates in the aggregate evidence the entire beneficial ownership in the Trust. &nbsp;The Certificates consist of the Classes set forth herein. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Pursuant to Section 12.01 of the Standard Terms, the Securities Administrator, on behalf of the Trustee, will make an election to treat all of the assets of the Trust as three real estate mortgage investment conduits (each, a &#147;<U>REMIC</U>&#148; and, individually, &#147;<U>REMIC I-1</U>,&#148; &#147;<U>REMIC I-2</U>&#148; and &#147;<U>REMIC I-3</U>&#148;) for federal income tax purposes. &nbsp;The &#147;startup day&#148; of each REMIC for purposes of the REMIC Provisions is the Closing Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">For purposes of naming the REMIC Interests and the Certificates, the first character (&#147;1,&#148; &#147;2,&#148; &#147;3,&#148; &#147;4,&#148; &#147;5,&#148; &#147;6,&#148; or &nbsp;&#147;7&#148;), if any, refers to the Collateral Group; the second character (&#147;A&#148; or &#147;B&#148;), if any, refers to the status of the interest (&#147;A&#148; for senior or &#147;B&#148; for subordinate) and the final character (&#147;1,&#148; &#147;2,&#148; &#147;3,&#148; &#147;4,&#148; &#147;5,&#148; &#147;6,&#148; &#147;P,&#148; &#147;R&#148; or &#147;X&#148;) refers to the specific Class.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual promises, covenants, representations and warranties hereinafter set forth, the Depositor, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Custodian and the Master Servicer agree as follows:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>ARTICLE I</B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767937"></A><A NAME="_Toc515364502"></A><A NAME="_Toc1422951"></A><A NAME="_Toc90824628"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>DEFINITIONS</B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767938"></A><A NAME="_Toc515364503"></A><A NAME="_Toc1422952"></A><A NAME="_Toc90824629"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Section 1.01</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Standard Terms.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Depositor, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Custodian and the Master Servicer acknowledge that the Standard Terms prescribe certain obligations of each such entity with respect to the Certificates. &nbsp;The Depositor, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Custodian and the Master Servicer agree to observe and perform such prescribed duties, responsibilities and obligations, pursuant to the terms and conditions thereof and of this Trust Agreement, and acknowledge that, except to the extent inconsistent with the provisions of this Trust Agreement, the Standard Terms are and shall be a part of this Trust Agreement to the same extent as if set forth herein in full.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Pursuant to Section 2.02(f) of the Standard Terms, the Depositor acknowledges the appointment of the Custodian and agrees to deliver, or cause to be delivered, to the Custodian all Mortgage Loan documents that are to be included in the Trustee Mortgage Loan File for each Mortgage Loan. &nbsp;The Depositor and the Custodian acknowledge that, pursuant to existing Custodial Agreements entered into between the Custodian and predecessors in interest of the Depositor, the Custodian previously acted as custodian for such predecessors in interest and that in connection with the formation of the Trust, the Depositor will assign each Custodial Agreement to the Trustee and cause a receipt to be issued in the name of the Trustee. &nbsp;</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767939"></A><A NAME="_Toc515364504"></A><A NAME="_Toc1422953"></A><A NAME="_Toc90824630"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Section 1.02</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Defined Terms.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Capitalized terms used but not defined herein shall have the respective meanings assigned to them in Section 1.01 of the Standard Terms or in the Sale and Servicing Agreements. &nbsp;In the event of a conflict between the Standard Terms and the Sale and Servicing Agreements, the Sale and Servicing Agreements shall govern. &nbsp;In addition, the following provisions shall govern the defined terms set forth below for this Trust Agreement:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>ABN AMRO</U>&#148;: &nbsp;ABN AMRO Mortgage Group, Inc., or any successor in interest.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Accrued Certificate Interest</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Interest to be distributed to each Class of Certificates on any Distribution Date consisting of the sum of (i) interest accrued during the related Interest Accrual Period at the applicable Certificate Rate for such Class of Certificates on the Certificate Balance (or Notional Amount) of such Class of Certificates immediately preceding such Distribution Date and (ii) accrued but unpaid Accrued Certificate Interest from prior Distribution Dates (on a cumulative basis, but without interest on such unpaid Accrued Certificate Interest). &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Aggregate Subordinate Percentage</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For any Certificate Group at any time, the sum of the Class Principal Balances of the Subordinate Certificates divided by the sum of the outstanding principal balances for all the Mortgage Loans in the related Collateral Groups (other than the Applicable Fractions thereof allocable to the Class A-P Certificates). &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Applicable Fraction</U>&#148;: For each Mortgage Loan and REMIC I-1, shall be calculated as follows: &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:-18pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Symbol; font-size:12pt">&#183;</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Apportioned Principal Balance</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For any Class of Subordinate Certificates and any Distribution Date, the Class Principal Balance of such Class immediately prior to such Distribution Date multiplied by a fraction, the numerator of which is the related Group Subordinate Amount for such date and the denominator of which is the sum of the Group Subordinate Amounts for such date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&#147;<U>Assignment Agreements</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each of: &nbsp;(i) the Assignment, Assumption and Recognition Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, by and among GSMC, the Depositor and ABN AMRO, as servicer, (ii) the Assignment, Assumption and Recognition Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, by and among the Trustee, the Depositor and ABN AMRO, as servicer, and as acknowledged and agreed to by Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, as master servicer, (iii) the Assignment, Assumption and Recognition Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, by and among GSMC, the Depositor and CitiMortgage, as servicer, (iv) the Assignment, Assumption and Recognition Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, by and among the Trustee, the Depositor and CitiMortgage, as servicer, and as acknowledged and agreed to by Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, as master servicer, (v) the Assignment,

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Available Distribution Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For any Distribution Date and any Collateral Group, the sum of the Applicable Fractions for each Mortgage Loan contributing to such Collateral Group of the following amounts:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-right:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(1)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-right:36pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the total amount of all cash received from or on behalf of the Mortgagors or advanced by the applicable Servicer (or the Master Servicer in the event the applicable Servicer fails to make such required advances, or by the Securities Administrator in the event the Master Servicer fails to make any such required advances, in each case pursuant to Section 3.05 of the Standard Terms) on the Mortgage Loans contributing to such Collateral Group and not previously distributed (including P&amp;I Advances made by such Servicer (or by the Master Servicer in the event the applicable Servicer fails to make such required advances, or by the Securities Administrator in the event the Master Servicer fails to make any such required advances, in each case pursuant to Section 3.05 of the Standard Terms), Compensating Interest Payments made by such Servicer (or th
e Master Servicer) and proceeds of Mortgage Loans that are liquidated), except:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(a)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">all Scheduled Payments collected but due on a Due Date after such Distribution Date;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(b)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">all Curtailments received after the previous calendar month;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(c)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">all Payoffs received after the previous calendar month (together with any interest payment received with such Payoffs to the extent that it represents the payment of interest accrued on the Mortgage Loans contributing to such Collateral Group for the period after the previous calendar month);</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(d)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Liquidation Proceeds, Condemnation Proceeds and Insurance Proceeds received on the Mortgage Loans contributing to such Collateral Group after the previous calendar month;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(e)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">all amounts in the Certificate Account from Mortgage Loans contributing to such Collateral Group that are then due and payable to the applicable Servicer under the related Sale and Servicing Agreement; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(f)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the Servicing Fee and the Master Servicing Fee for each Mortgage Loan in such Group, net of any amounts payable as compensating interest by the applicable Servicer on that Distribution Date; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(g)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">all related indemnification amounts and other amounts reimbursable on such Distribution Date to the Securities Administrator or the Trustee or the Master Servicer; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(h)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">all expenses of the Trust Fund paid after the immediately preceding Distribution Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(2)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the total amount of any cash received by the Securities Administrator or the applicable Servicer (or the Master Servicer) from the repurchase by the applicable Loan Seller of any Mortgage Loans contributing to such Collateral Group as a result of defective documentation or breach of representations and warranties (<I>provided</I> that the obligation to repurchase arose before the related Due Date); <I>provided further</I> that the Available Distribution Amount for REMIC I-3 shall be the amounts distributed by REMIC I-2 and the Available Distribution Amount for REMIC I-2 shall be the amounts distributed by REMIC I-1.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><I>provided that</I> interest with respect to any Mortgage Loan that relates to two Collateral Groups will be included in the Available Distribution Amount for each related Collateral Group as follows: <I>first</I>, to the Collateral Group with the lower Effective Net Rate, interest to the extent accrued on the Applicable Fraction of the principal of such Mortgage Loan at the Effective Net Rate for such Collateral Group; and <I>second</I>, to the other Collateral Group related to such Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<U>B Average Rate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For each Distribution Date, an annual rate equal to the weighted average of the Designated Rates applicable to each Collateral Group, weighted on the basis of the Group Subordinate Amounts for the Collateral Groups.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<U>BOA</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Bank of America, N.A., or any successor in interest.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Book-Entry Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The Senior Certificates and the Senior Subordinate Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Cendant</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Cendant Mortgage Corporation, or any successor in interest.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Certificate Balance</U>&#148;: &nbsp;As to any Class of Certificates (other than any Interest Only Certificate) or Interests as of the close of business on each Distribution Date, the initial Certificate Balance thereof &nbsp;(as shown on the charts in Section 2.03) reduced by (i) all principal payments previously distributed to such Class and (ii) all Realized Losses previously allocated to such Class and increased, in the case of the Class 2A-4 Certificates only, by interest accrued on such Class of Certificates before such Distribution Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Certificate Group</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The Group 1 Certificates, the Group 2 Certificates, the Group 3 Certificates, the Group 4 Certificates, the Group 5 Certificates, the Group 6 Certificates and the Group 7 Certificates, as applicable.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Certificate Rate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to each Class of Certificates on any Distribution Date, the percentage <I>per annum</I> or other entitlement to interest described in Section 2.03. &nbsp;With respect to each REMIC Interest on any Distribution Date, the Certificate Rates described in Section 2.03.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Class</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each Class of Certificates or REMIC Interests.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<U>Class A-X Notional Amoun</U>t&#148;: &nbsp;Initially will be $695,498.56 and for each Distribution Date after the Closing Date will equal to the sum of (a) the product of (1) a fraction, the numerator of which is the weighted average of the Net Rates of the Premium Loans in Loan Group I at the beginning of the related Due Period minus 8.00% and the denominator of which is 6.00% and (2) the total principal balance of the Premium Loans in Loan Group I as of the first day of the related Interest Accrual Period; (b) the product of (1) a fraction, the numerator of which is the weighted average of the Net Rates of the Premium Loans in Loan Group II at the beginning of the related Due Period minus 5.50% and the denominator of which is 6.00% and (2) the total principal balance of the Premium Loans in Loan Group II as of the first day of the related Interest Accrual Per
iod; and (c) the product of (1) a fraction, the numerator of which is the weighted average of the Net Rates of the Premium Loans in Loan Group III at the beginning of the related Due Period minus 7.50% and the denominator of which is 6.00% and (2) the total principal balance of the Premium Loans in Loan Group III as of the first day of the related Interest Accrual Period. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Class B Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The Class B1, Class B2, Class B3, Class B4, Class B5 and Class B6 Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Class 2A-3 Notional Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to each Distribution Date, (a) 1.00% of the Class Principal Balance of the Class 2A-2 Certificates on such Distribution Date, divided by (b) 6.00%.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Class 3A-2 Notional Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to each Distribution Date, the Class Principal Balance of the Class 3A-1 Certificates on such Distribution Date.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Closing Date</U>&#148;: &nbsp;December 17, 2004.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Credit Support Depletion Date</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The first Distribution Date (if any) on which the aggregate Certificate Balance of the Subordinate Certificates has been or will be reduced to zero.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Current Realized Loss</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For the Class A-P Certificates and each Distribution Date, the sum of the related Applicable Fraction of Realized Losses realized during the preceding calendar month on each Discount Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Current Shortfall</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any amount included in the Principal Distribution Amount for which cash is not available to make distributions as a result of the Servicer&#146;s decision not to Advance a delinquent payment, other than a Realized Loss.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Curtailment</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any partial prepayment on any Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Custodian</U>&#148;: &nbsp;JPMorgan Chase Bank, National Association in its capacity as custodian under the applicable Custodial Agreements.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Custodial Agreement</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each of (i) the Custodial Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, between Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, and JPMorgan Chase, as custodian, (ii) the Custodial Agreement, dated as of September 1, 2004, among Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, and JPMorgan Chase, as custodian, &nbsp;(iii) the Custodial Agreement, dated as of June 1, 2002, among Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, BOA, as seller, and JPMorgan Chase, as custodian, (iv) the Custodial Agreement, dated, as of July 1, 2004, among Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, Cendant, as seller, and JPMorgan Chase, as custodian, (v) the Bailee Agreement, dated as of July 2, 2004, among Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, JP Morgan Chase Bank and CMMC, (vi) the Custodial Agreement, dated as of October 1, 2004, among Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as
 purchaser, CitiMortgage, as servicer, and JPMorgan Chase, as custodian (vii) the Custodial Agreement, dated as of March 1, 2004 among Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, Countrywide, as seller, Countrywide Home Loans Servicing LP, as servicer, and JPMorgan Chase, as custodian, and (viii) the Custodial Agreement, dated as of October 1, 2004 among Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, WaMu, Washington Mutual Bank fsb and Washington Mutual Bank, as sellers, and JPMorgan Chase, as custodian.</P>

With respect to Collateral Group 2, 6.00% per annum. &nbsp;With respect to Collateral Group 3, 8.00% per annum. &nbsp;With respect to Collateral Group 4, 4.75% per annum. &nbsp;With respect to Collateral Group 5, 5.50% per annum. &nbsp;With respect to Collateral Group 6, 6.00% per annum. &nbsp;With respect to Collateral Group 7, 7.50% per annum. &nbsp;</P>

The initial Distribution Date will be December 27, 2004.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Due Date</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For any Mortgage Loan, the first day in each calendar month.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Due Period</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For any Distribution Date, the period beginning on the second day of the month immediately preceding the month in which such Distribution Date occurs and ending on the first day of the month in which such Distribution Date occurs.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group 1 Certificate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Class 1A-1, Class 1A-2, Class 1A-3 or Class 1A-4 Certificate.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group I NAS Percentage</U>&#148;: With respect to any Distribution Date, the lesser of (i) 100% and (ii) the percentage obtained by dividing (x) the aggregate Certificate Balance of the Class 1A-3 and Class 1A-4 Certificates immediately prior to such date by (y) the aggregate Certificate Balance of the Class 1A-1, Class 1A-2, Class 1A-3 and Class 1A-4 Certificates immediately prior to such date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group I NAS Prepayment Shift Percentage</U>&#148;: With respect to any Distribution Date during the five years beginning on the first Distribution Date, 0%. &nbsp;Thereafter, for any Distribution Date occurring on or after the fifth anniversary of the first Distribution Date, as follows: for any Distribution Date in the first year thereafter, 30%; for any Distribution Date in the second year thereafter, 40%; for any Distribution Date in the third year thereafter, 60%; for any Distribution Date in the fourth year thereafter, 80%; and for any subsequent Distribution Date, 100%.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group I NAS Priority Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to any Distribution Date, the lesser of (i) the sum of (x) the product of the Group I NAS Percentage for such date, the Group I NAS Scheduled Principal Percentage for such date and the Scheduled Principal Amount for such date and (y) the product of the Group I NAS Percentage for such date, the Group I NAS Prepayment Shift Percentage for such date and the Unscheduled Principal Amount for such date and (ii) the aggregate Certificate Balance of the Class 1A-3 and Class 1-A4 Certificates immediately prior to such date. &nbsp;Notwithstanding the foregoing, (i) on and after the Credit Support Depletion Date, the Class 1A-3 and Class 1A-4 Certificates shall be entitled to their respective pro rata share of all scheduled and unscheduled payments of principal and (ii) on the date on which the Certificate Balances of all of the
 Class 1A-1 and Class 1A-2 Certificates have been reduced to zero, the Class 1A-3 and Class 1A-4 Certificates shall be entitled pro rata to any remaining Senior Principal Distribution Amount for Collateral Group 1 and thereafter, the Group I NAS Priority Amount will equal the Senior Principal Distribution Amount for Collateral Group 1.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group I NAS Scheduled Principal Percentage</U>&#148;: With respect to any Distribution Date during the five years beginning on the first Distribution Date, 0%. &nbsp;Thereafter, for any Distribution Date occurring on or after the fifth anniversary of the first Distribution Date, 100%.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group 2 Certificate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Class 2A-1, Class 2A-2, Class 2A-3 or Class 2A-4 Certificate.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group 3 Certificate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Class 3A-1 or Class 3A-2.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group 4 Certificate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Class 4A-1 Certificate.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group 5 Certificate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Class 5A-1 Certificate.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group I Mortgage Loan</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Mortgage Loan in Loan Group I.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group II Mortgage Loan</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Mortgage Loan in Loan Group II.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group III Mortgage Loan</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Mortgage Loan in Loan Group III.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Group Subordinate Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to each Collateral Group and any Distribution Date, the excess of the sum of the Applicable Fractions of the outstanding Principal Balance of the Mortgage Loans contributing to such Collateral Group for the immediately preceding Distribution Date for such Collateral Group (other than the Applicable Fractions thereof allocable to the Class A-P Certificates) over the total Certificate Balance of the Senior Certificates of the related Certificate Group (other than the Class A-P Certificates) immediately prior to such Distribution Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>GSMC</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, or any successor in interest.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&#147;<U>Interest Accrual Period</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For any Distribution Date and any regular interest in REMIC I-1 or REMIC I-2 or any Class of Certificates other than the Class A-P, Class 3A-1, Class 3A-2, Class 7A-1 and Class 7A-2 Certificates, the calendar month immediately preceding the calendar month in which such Distribution Date occurs. &nbsp;For any Distribution Date and the Class 3A-1, Class 3A-2, Class 7A-1 and Class 7A-2 Certificates, the period from and including the 25th day of the month immediately preceding the month in which such Distribution Date occurs to and including the 24th day of the month in which such Distribution Date occurs. &nbsp;The Class A-P Certificates will be &#147;principal only&#148; Certificates and will not be entitled to any interest. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Interest Only Certificate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Class 2A-3, Class 3A-2, Class 7A-2 or Class A-X Certificate.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Interests</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each Class of REMIC Interests.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>JPMorgan Chase</U>&#148;: &nbsp;JPMorgan Chase Bank, National Association.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Junior Subordinate Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The Class B4, Class B5 and Class B6 Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>LIBOR</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Shall be 2.370% for the first Interest Accrual Period and, for any subsequent Interest Accrual Period, the offered rate for one-month United States dollar deposits which appears on Telerate Page 3750, as reported by Bloomberg Financial Markets Commodities News (or such other page as may replace Telerate Page 3750 for the purpose of displaying comparable rates), as of 11:00 a.m. (London time) on the LIBOR Determination Date applicable to such Interest Accrual Period. &nbsp;If such rate does not appear on Telerate Page 3750 (or such other page as may replace Telerate Page 3750 for the purpose of displaying comparable rates), the rate for that day will be determined on the basis of the rates at which deposits in United States dollars are offered by the Reference Banks at approximately 11:00 a.m., London time, on that day to leading banks in the London int
erbank market for a period of one month commencing on the first day of the relevant Interest Accrual Period. &nbsp;The Securities Administrator will request the principal London office of each of the Reference Banks to provide a quotation of its rate to the Securities Administrator. &nbsp;If at least two such quotations are provided, the rate for that day will be the arithmetic mean of the quotations. &nbsp;If fewer than two quotations are provided as requested, the rate for that day will be the arithmetic mean of the rates quoted by major banks in New York City, selected by the Securities Administrator, at approximately 11:00 a.m., New York City time, on that day for loans in United States dollars to leading European banks for a one-month period (commencing on the first day of the relevant Interest Accrual Period). &nbsp;If none of such major banks selected by the Securities Administrator quotes such rate to the Securities Administrator, LIBOR for such LIBOR Determination Date will be the rate in effect wit
h respect to the immediately preceding LIBOR Determination Date. &nbsp;The Securities Administrator&#146;s determination of LIBOR for any Determination Date and any Certificate Rate based on such LIBOR calculation shall be final and binding in the absence of manifest error.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>LIBOR Determination Date</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to any Interest Accrual Period and any floating rate certificate, the second London Business Day prior to the date on which such Interest Accrual Period commences.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Liquidation Principal</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The principal portion of Liquidation Proceeds received from each Mortgage Loan that became a Liquidated Mortgage Loan during the calendar month preceding the month of the Distribution Date. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Loan Group I</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The aggregate of the Mortgage Loans identified on Schedule I as being included in Loan Group I.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Loan Group II</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The aggregate of the Mortgage Loans identified on Schedule I as being included in Loan Group II.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Loan Group III</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The aggregate of the Mortgage Loans identified on Schedule I as being included in Loan Group III.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Loan Seller</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each of ABN AMRO, BOA, Cendant, Chase, CitiMortgage, Countrywide and WaMu.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Master Servicer</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, its successors and assigns, including any successor master servicer.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Master Servicing Fee</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to any Distribution Date, all income and gain realized from the investment of funds in the Master Servicer Account during the period from and including the Master Servicer Remittance Date in the calendar month immediately preceding the month in which such Distribution Date occurs, to but excluding the Master Servicer Remittance Date relating to such Distribution Date. &nbsp;Pursuant to a separate agreement, the Master Servicer will pay the Trustee fee and the Securities Administrator fee from the Master Servicing Fee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Moody&#146;s</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Moody&#146;s Investors Service, Inc.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Mortgage Loans</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The mortgage loans identified on Schedule I hereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Net Rate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to each Mortgage Loan, the Note Rate of such Mortgage Loan less the Servicing Fee Rate applicable to such Mortgage Loan. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Non-AP Pool Balance</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For any Distribution Date and any Collateral Group (other than Collateral Group P), the sum of the products, for each Mortgage Loan contributing to such Collateral Group, of (i) the Applicable Fraction for such Mortgage Loan in respect of such Collateral Group and (ii) the outstanding principal balance of such Mortgage Loan as of the Due Date of the month in which such Distribution Date occurs.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Note Rate</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For each Mortgage Loan, the rate at which the related promissory note accrues interest. &nbsp;For purposes of calculating the Certificate Rates on the Interests and Certificates, the Note Rate of a Mortgage Loan will be calculated without regard to any modification, waiver or amendment of the interest rate of the Mortgage Loan, whether agreed to by the Servicer or resulting from a bankruptcy, insolvency or similar proceeding involving the related Mortgagor. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Notional Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each of the Class 2A-3 Notional Amount, Class 3A-2 Notional Amount, Class 7A-2 Notional Amount and the Class A-X Notional Amount. &nbsp;Each Notional Amount is used to calculate distributions on the related Class of Certificates, but is not a principal amount or other amount to which a Certificateholder is entitled.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>P&amp;I Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;All Classes of Certificates other than the Class 2A-3, Class 3A-2, Class 7A-2, Class A-X, Class A-P Certificates and the Residual Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Payoffs</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any prepayment in full on any Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Premium Loan</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any Mortgage Loan in Loan Group I with a Net Rate greater than 8.00%, any Mortgage Loan in Loan Group II with a Net Rate greater than 5.50% and any Mortgage Loan in Loan Group III with a Net Rate greater than 7.50%.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Prepayment Period</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to each Distribution Date, the preceding calendar month.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Principal Distribution Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For each Collateral Group and any Distribution Date, the sum of:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(1)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the Principal Payment Amount for such Collateral Group;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(2)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the Principal Prepayment Amount for such Collateral Group; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(3)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the Applicable Fraction for each Mortgage Loan contributing to such Collateral Group of the Liquidation Principal derived from such Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Principal Payment Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For each Collateral Group (other than Collateral Group P) and any Distribution Date, the sum of the products, for each Mortgage Loan contributing to such Collateral Group, of (i) the Applicable Fraction for such Mortgage Loan in respect of such Collateral Group and (ii) the sum of the following amounts:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(1)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the principal portion of Scheduled Payments on such Mortgage Loan due on the related Due Date and received or advanced during the related Due Period; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(2)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the principal portion of repurchase proceeds received on such Mortgage Loan if such Mortgage Loan was repurchased as permitted or required by this Trust Agreement during the calendar month preceding the month of such Distribution Date; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(3)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">any other unscheduled payments of principal which were received on such Mortgage Loan during the preceding calendar month, other than Payoffs, Curtailments, or Liquidation Principal; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(4)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">current Realized Losses and Deferred Principal Amounts, to the extent of the amount available from the related Subordinate Principal Distribution Amount.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Principal Prepayment Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;&nbsp;For any Distribution Date and any Collateral Group (other than Collateral Group P), the sum of the products, for each Mortgage Loan contributing to such Collateral Group, of (i) the Applicable Fraction for such Mortgage Loan in respect of such Collateral Group and (ii) all Payoffs and Curtailments for such Mortgage Loan that were received during the preceding calendar month. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Private Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The Junior Subordinate Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Qualified Institutional Buyer</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Any &#147;qualified institutional buyer&#148; as defined in clause 7(a) of Rule 144A promulgated under the Securities Act.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Rating Agency</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each of Moody&#146;s and S&amp;P.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Record Date</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For each Class of Certificates, the last Business Day of the related Interest Accrual Period.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC</U>&#148;: &nbsp;REMIC I-1, REMIC I-2 or REMIC I-3. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each Class of Certificates issued by REMIC I-3 pursuant to Section 2.03 and the Class R Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC Interests</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each Class of REMIC interests issued pursuant to Section 2.03.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC I-1</U>&#148;: &nbsp;One of the three real estate mortgage investment conduits created hereunder, which consists of the Mortgage Loans and certain other assets and the REMIC I-1 Distribution Account.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC I-1 Regular Interests</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The regular interests issued by REMIC I-1 as specified in Section 2.03.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC I-2</U>&#148;: &nbsp;One of the three real estate mortgage investment conduits created hereunder, which consists of the REMIC I-1 Regular Interests and the REMIC I-2 Distribution Account.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC I-2 Regular Interests</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The regular interests issued by REMIC I-2 as specified in Section 2.03.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC I-3</U>&#148;: &nbsp;One of the three real estate mortgage investment conduits created hereunder, which consists of the REMIC I-2 Regular Interests and the Certificate Account.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>REMIC I-3 Regular Interests</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each Class of Certificates other than the Residual Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Remittance Date</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The 18<SUP>th</SUP> day of each month or if such day is not a Business Day, the preceding (or, in the case of certain Mortgage Loans serviced by BOA, Countrywide and WaMu, the next succeeding) Business Day, as set forth in the applicable Servicing Agreement. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Residual Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The Class R Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Rule 144A Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The Junior Subordinate Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>S&amp;P</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Standard &amp; Poor&#146;s Rating Services, a division of The McGraw-Hill Companies, Inc., or its successor.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Sale and Servicing Agreement</U>&#148;: &nbsp;Each of (i) the Amended and Restated Flow Sale, Warranties and Servicing Agreement, dated as of September 1, 2004, between Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, and ABN AMRO Mortgage Group Inc., as seller and servicer; (ii) the Mortgage Loan Sale and Servicing Agreement, dated as of June 1, 2002, between Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, and BOA, as seller and servicer; (iii) the Mortgage Loan Flow Purchase, Sale &amp; Servicing Agreement, dated as of June 1, 2004, between Cendant, Bishop&#146;s Gate Residential Mortgage Trust (formerly known as Cendant Residential Mortgage Trust), as seller and Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, as amended pursuant to Amendment No. 1 thereto, dated as of July 1, 2004; (iv) the Flow Mortgage Loan Purchase, Warranties and Servicing Agreement, dated as of April 1, 200
4, between Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, as servicer, and Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company; (v) the Mortgage Loan Purchase, Warranties and Servicing Agreement, dated as of August 1, 2002, between Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, and Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, as seller and servicer; (vi) the Flow Mortgage Loan Purchase and Servicing Agreement, dated as of October, 1, 2004, between Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser, and CitiMortgage, as seller and servicer; (vii) the Servicing Agreement, dated as of July 1, 2004, between Countrywide Home Loans Servicing, LP, as servicer, and Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as owner; (viii) the Master Mortgage Loan Purchase Agreement, dated as of July 1, 2004, between Countrywide, as seller, and Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as purchaser; (ix) the Mortgage Loan Purchase and Sale Agreement, dated as of March 1, 2004, among WaMu, Washington Mutual Bank fsb, and Washington Mutual Bank, as sellers, and Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company, as p
urchaser; and (x) the Servicing Agreement, dated as of December 1, 2003, between WaMu and Goldman Sachs Mortgage Company.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Scheduled Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to any Distribution Date and the Class 2A-2 Certificates, the amount set forth on Schedule II attached hereto for such Distribution Date and Class.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Scheduled Payments</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to any Mortgage Loan, the monthly payments of principal and interest payable by the Mortgagor pursuant to the related amortization schedule. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Scheduled Principal Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;With respect to any Distribution Date an amount equal to the amount described in clause (i) of the definition of Senior Principal Distribution Amount. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Securities Administrator</U>&#148;: &nbsp;JPMorgan Chase in its capacity as Securities Administrator under this Trust Agreement, or its successor in interest in such capacity.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Senior Certificates</U>&#148;: &nbsp;The Class A Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Senior Collateral Group Percentage</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For Collateral Group 1, Collateral Group 2, Collateral Group 3, Collateral Group 4, Collateral Group 5, Collateral Group 6 and Collateral Group 7 will equal (i) as of the Closing Date, 97.10%, 97.10%, 97.10%, 98.55%, 98.55%, 98.53% and 98.54%, respectively, and (ii) for any Distribution Date thereafter will be a fraction expressed as a percentage equal to (a) the sum of the Certificate Balances of the Senior Certificates related to such Collateral Group (other than the Class A-P Certificates) immediately preceding such Distribution Date, over (b) the sum of the products, for each Mortgage Loan contributing to such Collateral Group, of (x) the Applicable Fraction for such Mortgage Loan in respect of such Collateral Group and (y) the outstanding principal balance of such Mortgage Loan as of the Due Date of the month in which 
such Distribution Date occurs.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Senior Interests</U>&#148;: &nbsp;All of the REMIC I-2 Regular Interests except those corresponding to a Class B Certificate.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Senior Liquidation Amount</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For any Distribution Date and any Collateral Group (other than Collateral Group P), the aggregate, for each Mortgage Loan contributing to such Collateral Group that became a Liquidated Mortgage Loan during the calendar month preceding the month of such Distribution Date, of the related Senior Collateral Group Percentage of the lesser of the Applicable Fraction of (i) the scheduled principal balance of such Mortgage Loan and (ii) the Liquidation Principal derived from such Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&#147;<U>Senior</U><I><U> </U></I><U>Prepayment</U><I><U> </U></I><U>Percentage</U>&#148;: &nbsp;For each Collateral Group, as follows: &nbsp;(i) on any Distribution Date occurring before the Distribution Date in the month of December 2009, 100%; (ii) on any other Distribution Date on which the related Senior Collateral Group Percentage for such Distribution Date exceeds the initial Senior Collateral Group Percentage as of the Cut-Off Date, 100% (in which case, the Senior Prepayment Percentage for each other Collateral Group shall also equal 100% for such Distribution Date); and (iii) on any other Distribution Date in the month of December 2009 and thereafter, 100%, unless:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(a)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the mean of the sum of the Applicable Fractions of the Scheduled Principal Balances of the Mortgage Loans contributing to each Collateral Group that are 60 or more days delinquent (including Mortgage Loans in foreclosure or bankruptcy and property held by the Trust) for each of the immediately preceding three calendar months is less than or equal to 50% of the Group Subordinate Amount for such Collateral Group as&nbsp;of such Distribution Date, and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(b)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">the sum of the Applicable Fractions of the cumulative Realized Losses on the Mortgage Loans contributing to each Collateral Group are less than or equal to the following percentage of the aggregate Group Subordinate Amount for such Collateral Group:</P>
