<A NAME="_Toc515885706"></A><A NAME="_Toc90824671"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman Bold; font-size:12pt"><B>Section 1.01</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman Bold; font-size:12pt"><B>Defined Terms.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Except as otherwise specified herein or in the Trust Agreement or as the context may otherwise require, whenever used in these Standard Terms, the following words and phrases shall have the meanings specified in this Article. &nbsp;Capitalized words and phrases used herein but not defined herein shall, when applied to a Trust, have the meanings set forth in the Servicing Agreement(s) assigned to such Trust as in effect on the date of this Agreement. &nbsp;Unless otherwise specified, all calculations described herein shall be made on the basis of a 360-day year consisting of twelve 30-day months.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Accounting Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to each Distribution Date, the last day of the month preceding the month in which such Distribution Date occurs.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Administrative Cost Rate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Not applicable.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Advance&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The aggregate amount of the (i)&nbsp;advances made by a Servicer on any Servicer Remittance Date in respect of delinquent Monthly Payments pursuant to the applicable Sale and Servicing Agreement, (ii)&nbsp;any advances made by the Master Servicer (or by the Securities Administrator pursuant to Section 3.05 in the event the Master Servicer fails to make such advances as required) in respect of any such delinquent Monthly Payment pursuant to Section&nbsp;3.06 and (iii)&nbsp;amounts necessary to preserve the Trust&#146;s interest in the Mortgaged Premises or the Mortgage Loans, including without limitation, property taxes or insurance premiums not paid as required by the Mortgagor and advanced by the related Servicer or the Master Servicer (or by the Securities Administrator pursuant to Section 3.05 in the event the Master Servicer fails to make 
such advances as required).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Affiliate&#148;</I></B>: Any person or entity controlling, controlled by, or under common Control with the Depositor, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Custodian, the Master Servicer or any Servicer. &nbsp;&#147;Control&#148; means the power to direct the management and policies of a person or entity, directly or indirectly, whether through ownership of voting securities, by contract or otherwise. &nbsp;&#147;Controlling&#148; and &#147;controlled&#148; shall have meanings correlative to the foregoing.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Aggregate Principal Distribution Amount&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The amount specified in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;ARM Loan&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An &#147;adjustable rate&#148; Mortgage Loan, the Note Rate of which is subject to periodic adjustment in accordance with the terms of the Note.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Assignment Agreement&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any Assignment, Assumption and Recognition Agreement or Agreements identified in the Trust Agreement to which the Depositor is a party.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Available Distribution Amount&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Unless otherwise provided in the Trust Agreement, on each Distribution Date the Available Distribution Amount shall equal (i)&nbsp;the sum of the following: &nbsp;(A)&nbsp;all amounts credited to the Collection Account as of the close of business on the related Distribution Date, (B)&nbsp;an amount equal to Monthly Advances made on or before the previous Distribution Date, to the extent such Monthly Advance was made from funds on deposit in any related Collection Account held for future distribution, (C)&nbsp; all Monthly Advances made with respect to such Distribution Date (to the extent not included in clause&nbsp;(B)&nbsp;above) and (D)&nbsp;all amounts deposited into the Certificate Account to effect a Terminating Purchase in accordance with Section&nbsp;10.02 <I>minus</I> (ii)&nbsp;the sum of &nbsp;(A)&nbsp;any Princ
ipal Prepayments (including Liquidation Proceeds, Insurance Proceeds and Condemnation Proceeds) or Payoffs received after the related Principal Prepayment Period, (B)&nbsp;Monthly Payments collected but due on a Due Date or Dates subsequent to the related Due Period and (C)&nbsp;reinvestment income on amounts deposited in any Collection Account to the extent included in (i) above.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Bankruptcy Loss&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any reduction in the total amount owed by a Borrower on a Mortgage Loan occurring as a result of a final order of a court in a bankruptcy proceeding.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Beneficial Owner&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to a Book-Entry Security, the Person who is registered as owner of that Certificate in the books of the Clearing Agency for that Certificate or in the books of a Person maintaining an account with such Clearing Agency.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Benefit Plan Affidavit&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An affidavit substantially in the form of <U>Exhibit&nbsp;E</U> hereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Benefit Plan Opinion&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An opinion of counsel satisfactory to the Trustee and the Securities Administrator (and upon which the Trustee, the Master Servicer, the Securities Administrator and the Depositor shall be entitled to rely) to the effect that the purchase or holding of such Certificate by the prospective transferee will not result in any non-exempt prohibited transactions under Section 406 of ERISA or Section 4975 of the Code and will not subject the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer or the Depositor to any obligation in addition to those undertaken by such parties in the Trust Agreement, which opinion of counsel shall not be an expense of the Trust or any of the above parties. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Bond Level Reports</I>&#148;</B>: &nbsp;Shall mean the reports prepared by the Securities Administrator in substantially the form attached as Schedule&nbsp;I hereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Book-Entry Custodian&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The custodian appointed pursuant to Section&nbsp;5.03(d).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Book-Entry Securities&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Classes of Certificates, if any, specified as such in the Trust Agreement for a Series.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Borrower&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The individual or individuals obligated to repay a Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Business Day&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any day that is not (i)&nbsp;a Saturday or Sunday, or (ii)&nbsp;a legal holiday in the State of New York and the state in which the Corporate Trust Office or the principal offices of the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer or any Servicer are located, or (iii)&nbsp;a day on which the banking or savings and loan institutions in the State of New York and the state in which the Corporate Trust Office or the principal office of the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer or any Servicer is located are authorized or obligated by law or executive order to be closed.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Certificate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any security issued under the Trust Agreement and designated as such.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767122"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Certificate Account&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The account or accounts created and maintained for a Trust pursuant to Section&nbsp;3.01 hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Certificate Balance&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to each Class of Certificates or Interests, as of the close of business on any Distribution Date, the initial balance of such Class of Certificates or Interests set forth in the Trust Agreement reduced by (a)&nbsp;all principal payments previously distributed to such Class of Certificates or Interests in accordance with the Trust Agreement, and (b)&nbsp;all Realized Losses, if any, previously allocated to such Class of Certificates or Interests pursuant to the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Certificate of Title Insurance&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A certificate of title insurance issued pursuant to a master title insurance policy.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Certificate Rate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to the Certificates, as to each Distribution Date, the rate specified as such in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767123"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Certificate Register&#148;</I></B> and <B><I>&#147;Certificate Registrar&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The register maintained and the registrar appointed pursuant to Section&nbsp;5.04<A NAME="_Toc449767124"></A> hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Certificated Subordinated Certificates&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Classes of Certificates, if any, specified as such in the Trust Agreement for a Series.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Class&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Collectively, all of the Certificates bearing the same designation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Class B Interests&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;As set forth in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Clearing Agency&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Depository Trust Company, or any successor organization or any other organization registered as a &#147;clearing agency&#148; pursuant to Section&nbsp;17A of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, and the regulations of the Securities and Exchange Commission thereunder.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Clearing Agency Participant&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A broker, dealer, bank, other financial institution or other Person for whom from time to time a Clearing Agency effects book-entry transfers and pledges of securities deposited with the Clearing Agency.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Closing Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The date on which Certificates are issued by a Trust as set forth in the related Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Code&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Collection Account&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The collection account or accounts identified in or established in connection with the Servicing Agreement or Agreements identified in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Compensating Interest Payment&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to the Mortgage Loans and any Distribution Date, an amount equal to the excess of (x) the aggregate of any Prepayment Interest Shortfalls with respect to the Mortgage Loans and such Distribution Date over (y) the aggregate of any amounts required to be paid by any Servicer in respect of such shortfalls but not paid; provided that the aggregate Compensating Interest Payment to be paid by the Master Servicer for any Distribution Date shall not exceed the Master Servicing Fee that would be payable to the Master Servicer in respect of the Mortgage Loans and Distribution Date without giving effect to any Compensating Interest Payment.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Condemnation Proceeds&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;All awards or settlements in respect of a taking of an entire Mortgaged Premises or a part thereof by exercise of the power of eminent domain or condemnation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&nbsp;&#147;Contract of Insurance Holder&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any FHA approved mortgagee identified as such in the Trust Agreement or any Servicing Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Contractually Delinquent&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to any Mortgage Loan, having one or more uncured delinquencies in respect of payment at any time during the term of such Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Corporate Trust Office&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The respective principal corporate trust office of the Trustee or the Securities Administrator, as applicable, at which at any particular time its corporate trust business shall be administered.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Custody Agreement&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Custody Agreement or Agreements identified in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Custodian&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Custodian or Custodians identified in the Trust Agreement, which shall hold all or a portion of the Trustee Mortgage Loan Files with respect to a Series.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Cut-off Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The date specified as such in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Defect Discovery Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to a Mortgage Loan, the date on which any of the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer or the Servicer first discovers a Qualification Defect affecting the Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Depositor&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;GS Mortgage Securities Corp., a Delaware corporation, and its successors.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767034"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Disqualified Organization&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Either (a)&nbsp;the United States, (b)&nbsp;any state or political subdivision thereof, (c)&nbsp;any foreign government, (d)&nbsp;any international organization, (e)&nbsp;any agency or instrumentality of any of the foregoing, (f)&nbsp;any tax-exempt organization (other than a cooperative described in Section&nbsp;521 of the Code) that is exempt from federal income tax unless such organization is subject to tax under the unrelated business taxable income provisions of the Code, (g)&nbsp;any organization described in Section&nbsp;1381(a)(2)(C) of the Code, or (h)&nbsp;any other entity identified as a disqualified organization by the REMIC Provisions. &nbsp;A corporation will not be treated as an instrumentality of the United States or any state or political subdivision thereof if all of its activitie
s are subject to tax and, with the exception of the Federal Home Loan Mortgage Corporation, a majority of its board of directors is not selected by such government<A NAME="_Toc449767035"></A>al unit.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Disqualified Organization Affidavit&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An affidavit substantially in the form of <U>Exhibit&nbsp;<A NAME="_Toc449767036"></A>F-2</U>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Distribution Account</I>&#148;</B>: An Eligible Account maintained by the Securities Administrator on behalf of the Trustee for the REMIC. &nbsp;Unless otherwise provided in the Trust Agreement, the Distribution Account shall be considered an asset of the REMIC.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767037"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Distribution Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;<A NAME="_Toc449767038"></A>Shall have the meaning set forth in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Distribution Statement&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;As defined in Section&nbsp;4.01.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Due Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The first day of a calendar month.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Due Period&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to any Distribution Date, the period commencing on the second day of the calendar month preceding the calendar month in which such Distribution Date occurs and continuing through the first day of the month in which such Distribution Date<A NAME="_Toc449767040"></A> occurs.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Eligible Account&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A trust account (i)&nbsp;maintained by a depository institution, the long-term unsecured debt obligations are rated by the Rating Agency in one of its two highest rating categories at the time of any deposit therein, (ii)&nbsp;maintained with the Securities Administrator or the Trustee and satisfies either clause (i) or (iii) hereof or (iii)&nbsp;an account otherwise acceptable to the Rating Agency. &nbsp;If the definition of Eligible Account is met, any Certificate Account may be maintained with the Trustee, the Securities Administrator or the Master Servicer or any of their respective affiliates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;ERISA&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974, as <A NAME="_Toc449767042"></A>amended.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Errors and Omissions Insurance Policy&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An errors and omissions insurance policy to be maintained by the Master Servicer pursuant to Section 8.02 or a Servicer pursuant to the related Servicing Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Event of Default<A NAME="_Toc449767043"></A>&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to each Servicer, a Servicer Event of Default and with respect to the Master Servicer, a Master Servicer Event of Default.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Exchange Act&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Fidelity Bond&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A fidelity bond to be maintained by the Master Servicer pursuant to Section 8.02 or a Servicer pursuant to the related Servicing Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Final Certification&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A certification as to the completeness of each Trustee Mortgage Loan File substantially in the form of <U>Exhibit&nbsp;B</U> hereto provided by the Securities Administrator (or the Custodian) on or before the first anniversary of the Closing Date pursuant to Section&nbsp;2.02<A NAME="_Toc449767044"></A> hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Fiscal Year&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Unless otherwise provided in the Trust Agreement, the fiscal year of the Trust shall run from January 1 (or from the Closing Date, in the case of the first fiscal year) through the last day of<A NAME="_Toc449767045"></A> December.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Fraud Losses&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Losses on Mortgage Loans resulting from fraud, dishonesty or misrepresentation in the origination of such Mortgag<A NAME="_Toc449767046"></A>e Loans.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;GSMC&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Goldman Sachs Mortgage <A NAME="_Toc449767047"></A>Company, and its successors and assigns.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767050"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Holders&#148;</I></B> or <B><I>&#147;Certificateholders&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The holders of the Certificates, as shown on the &nbsp;Certificate Register maintained by the <A NAME="_Toc449767051"></A>Trustee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Independent&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;When used with respect to any specified Person, another Person who (a)&nbsp;is in fact independent of the Depositor, the Initial Purchaser, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer, each Servicer or GSMC, any obligor upon the Certificates or any Affiliate of the Depositor, the Initial Purchaser, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer, each Servicer or GSMC or such obligor, (b)&nbsp;does not have any direct financial interest or any material indirect financial interest in the Depositor, the Initial Purchaser, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer, each Servicer or &nbsp;GSMC or in any such obligor or in an Affiliate of the Depositor, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer, each Servicer or GSMC or such obligor, and (c)&nbsp;is not connected with t
he Depositor, the Initial Purchaser, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer, each Servicer or GSMC or any such obligor as an officer, employee, promoter, underwriter, trustee, partner, director or person performing similar functions. &nbsp;Whenever it is provided herein that any Independent Person&#146;s opinion or certificate shall be furnished to the Trustee or the Securities Administrator, such Person shall be appointed by the Depositor, the Initial Purchaser, the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer, any applicable Servicer or GSMC in the exercise of reasonable care by such Person, as the case may be, and approved by the Securities Administrator, and such opinion or certificate shall state that the Person executing the same has read this definition and that such Person is independent within the meaning t<A NAME="_Toc449767052"></A>hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Initial Certificate Balance&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to any Certificate or Class of Certificates, the Certificate Balance of such Certificate or Class of Certificates as of the Closing Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Initial Purchaser&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Goldman, Sac<A NAME="_Toc449767053"></A>hs &amp; Co.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Insurance Proceeds&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Proceeds of any Federal Insurance, title policy, hazard policy or other insurance policy covering a Mortgage Loan, if any, to the extent such proceeds are not to be applied to the restoration of the related Mortgaged Property or released to the Mortgagor in accordance with the procedures that the related Servicer would follow in servicing mortgage loans held for its own account.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Insurer&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any issuer of an insurance policy relating to the Mortgage Loans or Certificates of a<A NAME="_Toc449767054"></A> Series.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Interest&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The REMIC interests that are established by the Trust for purposes of the REMIC Provisions. &nbsp;The Interests shall be Regular Interests in, and assets of, the REMICs specified in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767055"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;JPMorgan Chase&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;JPMorgan Chase Bank, National Association and its successors.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Liquidated Mortgage Loan&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any Mortgage Loan for which the applicable Servicer has determined (and reported to the Master Servicer) that it has received all amounts that it expects to recover from or on account of such Mortgage Loan, whether from Insurance Proceeds, Liquidation Proceeds or otherwise.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Liquidation Loss&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to any Liquidated Mortgage Loan, the excess of (a) the sum of (i) the outstanding principal balance of such Mortgage Loan, (ii) all accrued and unpaid interest thereon, and (iii) the amount of all Advances and other expenses incurred with respect to such Mortgage Loan (including expenses of enforcement and foreclosure) over (b) Liquidation Proceeds realized from such Mortgage Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Liquidation Proceeds&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Amounts, other than Insurance Proceeds and Condemnation Proceeds, received by the related Servicer in connection with the liquidation of a defaulted Mortgage Loan through trustee&#146;s sale, foreclosure sale or otherwise, including amounts received following the disposition of an REO Property pursuant to the applicable Servicing Agreement less costs and expenses of such foreclosure sale.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Loan Level Report&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Shall mean the report prepared by the Master Servicer in substantially the form set forth in Schedule II hereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Loan-to-Value Ratio&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;For purposes of the REMIC Provisions, the ratio that results when the Unpaid Principal Balance of a Mortgage Loan is divided by the fair market value of the Mortgaged Premises (or, in the case of a Mortgage Loan that is secured by a leasehold interest, the fair market value of the leasehold interest and any improvements thereon). &nbsp;For purposes of determining that ratio, the fair market value of the Mortgaged Premises (or leasehold interest, as the case may be) must be reduced by (i)&nbsp;the full amount of any lien on the Mortgaged Premises (or leasehold interest, as the case may be) that is senior to the Mortgage Loan and (ii)&nbsp;a pro rata portion of any lien that is in parity with the Mortga<A NAME="_Toc449767056"></A>ge Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Lost Document Affidavit&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An affidavit, in recordable form, in which the Seller of a Mortgage Loan represents, warrants and covenants that: (i)&nbsp;immediately prior to the transfer of such Mortgage Loan under the related Sale Agreement, such Seller was the lawful owner of the Mortgage Loan and the Seller has not canceled, altered, assigned or hypothecated the mortgage note or the related Mortgage, (ii)&nbsp;the missing document was not located after a thorough and diligent search by the Seller, (iii)&nbsp;in the event that the missing document ever comes into the Seller&#146;s possession, custody or power, the Seller covenants immediately and without further consideration to surrender such document to the Securities Administrator, and (iv)&nbsp;that it shall indemnify and hold harmless the Trust, its successors, and assigns, against any loss, liabilit
y, or damage, including reasonable attorney&#146;s fees, resulting from the unavailability of any originals of any such documents or of a complete chain of intervening endorsements, as the case<A NAME="_Toc449767057"></A> may be.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Master Servicer&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Shall have the meaning set forth in the recitals hereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Master Servicer Account&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An Eligible Account established by the Master Servicer pursuant to Section&nbsp;3.01 hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Master Servicer Event of Default&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Those events of default described in Section&nbsp;8.04 hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Master Servicer Fee&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Shall have the meaning set forth in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Master Servicer Fee Rate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Not applicable.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Master Servicer Remittance Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to each Distribution Date, shall be a date which occurs two Business Days prior to such Distribution Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Modification Loss&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A decrease in the total payments due from a Borrower as a result of a modification of such Mortgage Loans following a default or reasonably expected default thereon. &nbsp;If a Modification Loss results in a decrease in the Note Rate of a Mortgage Loan, such Modification Loss shall be treated as occurring on each Due Date to the extent of such decrease.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Month End Interest Shortfall&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;For any Distribution Date, the aggregate Prepayment Interest Shortfall Amount for the Mortgage Loans, to the extent not paid out of the Servicer&#146;s Servicing Fee pursuant to the applicable Servicing Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767058"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Monthly Advance&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The aggregate amount of the (i)&nbsp;advances made by a Servicer on any Servicing Remittance Date in respect of delinquent Monthly Payments pursuant to the applicable Servicing Agreement and (ii)&nbsp;any advances made by the Master Servicer (or the Securities Administrator pursuant to Section 3.05 in the event the Master Servicer fails to make such advances as required) in respect of any such delinquent Monthly Payment pursuant to Section&nbsp;3.05.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Monthly Payment&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to any Mortgage Loan, the scheduled monthly payment of principal thereof and interest thereon due in any month under the terms <A NAME="_Toc449767059"></A>thereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Mortgage Loan&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The mortgage loans sold by the Depositor to the Trust as listed on the Mortgage Loan Schedule to the Trust Agreement. &nbsp;Unless the context indicates otherwise the term &#147;Mortgage Loan&#148; includes any REO Property held by th<A NAME="_Toc449767060"></A>e Trust.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Mortgage Loan Schedule&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The list of Mortgage Loans sold by the Depositor to the Trust, which Schedule is attached to the Trust Agreement and to the applicable Custody Agreement, and which shall set forth for each Mortgage Loan the following information:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(a) &nbsp;the Servicer (Depositor) loan number;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(b) &nbsp;the Borrower&#146;s name;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(c) &nbsp;the original principal balance;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(d) &nbsp;the Scheduled Principal Balance as of the close of business on the Cut off Date;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(e) &nbsp;the maturity date of the mortgage loan; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(f) &nbsp;the mortgage loan interest rate;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">together with such additional information as may be reasonably requested by the Securities Administrator or the Master Servicer.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Mortgaged Premises&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The real property securing repayment of the debt evidenced by a Note.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Mortgagor&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Borrower.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Net Rate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Unless otherwise provided in the Trust Agreement, with respect to each Mortgage Loan, the Note Rate of that Mortgage Loan less the Administrative Cost Rate applicable <A NAME="_Toc449767063"></A>thereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Non-U.S. Person&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A foreign person within the meaning of Treasury Regulation Section&nbsp;1.860G-3(a)(1) (<I>i.e.</I>, a person other than (i)&nbsp;a citizen or resident of the United States, (ii)&nbsp;a corporation or partnership that is organized under the laws of the United States or any jurisdiction thereof or therein, (iii)&nbsp;an estate that is subject to United States federal income tax regardless of the source of its income or (iv)&nbsp;a trust if a court within the United States is able to exercise primary supervision over the administration of such trust and one or more United States Persons have the authority to control all substantial decisions of the trust) who would be subject to United States income tax withholding pursuant to Section&nbsp;1441 or 1442 of the Code on income derived from the Residual Certificates<A NAME="_Toc449767064"></
A>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Non-U.S. Person Affidavit&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An affidavit substantially in the form of <U>Exhibit&nbsp;G-1<A NAME="_Toc449767065"></A></U> hereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Note&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A manually executed written instrument evidencing the Borrower&#146;s promise to repay a stated sum of money, <I>plus</I> interest, to the holder of the Note by a specific date according to a schedule of principal and interest p<A NAME="_Toc449767066"></A>ayments.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Note Rate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The rate of interest borne by each Note according to its terms.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767067"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Opinion of Counsel&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A written opinion of counsel, who may be counsel for the Depositor or a Servicer, acceptable to the Trustee, the Securities Administrator, the Master Servicer and the Servicer, as applicable. &nbsp;An Opinion of Counsel relating to tax matters must be an opinion of Independent <A NAME="_Toc449767068"></A>counsel.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767069"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Paying Agent&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The paying agent appointed pursuant to Section&nbsp;5.08<A NAME="_Toc449767070"></A> hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Payoff&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any payment or other recovery of principal on a Mortgage Loan equal to the Unpaid Principal Balance of &nbsp;such Mortgage Loan, received in advance of the last scheduled Due Date, including any prepayment penalty or premium thereon, which is accompanied by an amount of interest representing scheduled interest from the Due Date interest was last paid by the Mortgagor to the date of such prepayment.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Percentage Interest&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to any Certificate to which principal is assigned as of the Closing Date, the portion of the Class evidenced by such Certificate, expressed as a percentage, the numerator of which is the initial Certificate Balance of such Certificate and the denominator of which is the aggregate Certificate Balance of all of the Certificates of such Class as of the Closing Date. &nbsp;With respect to any Certificate to which a principal balance is not assigned as of the Closing Date, the portion of the Class evidenced by such Certificate, expressed as a percentage, as stated on the face of such Certificate<A NAME="_Toc449767071"></A>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Permitted Investments&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Permitted Investments shall consist of the following:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(i) &nbsp;direct obligations of, or obligations fully guaranteed as to principal and interest by, the United States or any agency or instrumentality thereof, provided such obligations are backed by the full faith and credit of the United States;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(ii) &nbsp;repurchase obligations (the collateral for which is held by a third party, the Trustee or the Securities Administrator, or any of their respective affiliates) with respect to any security described in clause&nbsp;(i) above, provided that the long-term or short-term unsecured debt obligations of the party agreeing to repurchase such obligations are at the time rated by each Rating Agency in its highest long-term unsecured debt rating categories;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(iii) &nbsp;certificates of deposit, time deposits and bankers&#146; acceptances of any bank or trust company (including the Trustee or the Securities Administrator) incorporated under the laws of the United States or any state, provided that the long-term unsecured debt obligations of such bank or trust company at the date of acquisition thereof have been rated by each Rating Agency in one of its two highest long-term unsecured debt rating categories;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(iv) &nbsp;commercial paper (having original maturities of not more than 270 days) of any corporation (including an affiliate of the Trustee or the Securities Administrator) incorporated under the laws of the United States or any state thereof which on the date of acquisition has been rated by each Rating Agency in its highest short-term unsecured debt rating available (<I>i.e.</I>, &#147;P-1&#148; by Moody&#146;s Investors Service, Inc. &#147;A-1+&#148; by Standard &amp; Poor&#146;s Ratings Services and &#147;F-1+&#148; by Fitch, Inc.);</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(v) &nbsp;money market funds administered by the Trustee or the Securities Administrator or any of their respective affiliates provided that such money market funds are rated by each Rating Agency &nbsp;(i)&nbsp;in its highest short-term unsecured debt rating category available (i.e., &#147;P-1&#148; by Moody&#146;s Investors Service, Inc. &#147;A-1+&#148; by Standard &amp; Poor&#146;s Ratings Services and &#147;F-1+&#148; by Fitch, Inc.) or (ii)&nbsp;in one of its two highest long-term unsecured debt rating categories; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(vi) &nbsp;any other demand, money market or time deposit or obligation, or interest-bearing or other security or investment as would not affect the then current rating of the Certificates by any Rating Agency (which shall include money market funds rated in the highest long-term rating category with portfolios consisting solely of obligations in clauses&nbsp;(i) through (iv) above);</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><I>provided, however,</I> that no investment described above shall constitute a Permitted Investment (A)&nbsp;if such investment evidences either the right to receive (i)&nbsp;only interest with respect to the obligations underlying such instrument or (ii)&nbsp;both principal and interest payments derived from obligations underlying such instrument if the interest and principal payments with respect to such instrument provide a yield to maturity at par greater than 120% of the yield to maturity at par of the underlying obligations or (B)&nbsp;if such investment is not a &#147;permitted investment&#148; for purposes of the REMIC Provisions; and <I>provided further,</I> that no investment described above shall constitute a Permitted Investment unless such investment matures no later than the Business Day immediately preceding the Distribution Date or the Master Servicer Remittance Date
, as applicable, on which the funds invested therein are required to be distributed (or, in the case of an investment that is an obligation of the institution in which the account is maintained, no later than such Distributio<A NAME="_Toc449767072"></A>n Date). &nbsp;Neither the Securities Administrator nor the Master Servicer shall sell or permit the sale of any Permitted Investment unless they shall have determined that such a sale would not result in a prohibited transaction in which a gain would be realized under the REMIC Provisions.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Person&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any individual, corporation, partnership, limited liability company, joint venture, association, joint stock company, trust (including any beneficiary thereof), unincorporated organization or government or any agency or political subdivision <A NAME="_Toc449767073"></A>thereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Plan&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any employee benefit plan or retirement arrangement, including individual retirement accounts and annuities, Keogh plans and collective investment funds in which such plans, accounts, annuities or arrangements are invested, that are described in or subject to the Plan Asset Regulations, ERISA or corresponding provisions of t<A NAME="_Toc449767074"></A>he Code.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Plan Asset Regulations&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Department of Labor regulations set forth in 29 C.F.R. &#167; 2510.3-101, as amended from time <A NAME="_Toc449767075"></A>to time.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Plan Investor&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any Plan, any Person acting on behalf of a Plan or any Person using the assets of<A NAME="_Toc449767076"></A> a Plan.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767078"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Prepayment Period&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Unless otherwise specified in the Trust Agreement, with respect to each Distribution Date, the calendar month preceding the month in which such Distribution Date <A NAME="_Toc449767079"></A>occurs.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Prepayment Interest Shortfall&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to any Distribution Date and (x) any Principal Prepayment Amount, the difference between (i) one full month&#146;s interest at the applicable Note Rate (after giving effect to any applicable Relief Act Reduction), as reduced by the applicable Servicing Fee Rate on the outstanding principal balance of such Mortgage Loan immediately prior to such prepayment and (ii) the amount of interest actually received with respect to such Mortgage Loan in connection with such Principal Prepayment Amount.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Prime Rate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to any Distribution Date, the rate published as the &#147;Prime Rate&#148; in the &#147;Money Rates&#148; Section&nbsp;or other comparable Section&nbsp;of <I>The Wall Street Journal</I> on such date. &nbsp;In the event <I>The Wall Street Journal</I> publishes a prime rate range, the average of that range, as determined by the Securities Administrator, shall be the Prime Rate. &nbsp;In the event <I>The Wall Street Journal</I> no longer publishes a &#147;Prime Rate&#148; entry, the Securities Administrator shall designate a new methodology for determining the Prime Rate based on comparable data.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767080"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Principal Prepayment Amount&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;As defined in the Trust Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767081"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Private Residual Certificate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any Class of Certificates designated as such in the Trust Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767082"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Private Certificate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any Class of Certificates designated as such in the Trust Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767083"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Purchase Price&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to a Mortgage Loan purchased from the Trust, an amount equal to the Scheduled Principal Balance of the Mortgage Loan, <I>plus</I> accrued and unpaid interest thereon at the Note Rate to the last day of the month in which the purchase occurs, <I>plus</I> the amount of any costs and damages incurred by the Trust as a result of any violation of any applicable federal, state, or local predatory or abusive lending law arising from or in connection with the origination of such Mortgage Loan, and <I>less</I> any amounts received in respect of such Mortgage Loan and being held in the Collection<A NAME="_Toc449767084"></A> Account.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Purchaser&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Person that purchases a Mortgage Loan from the Trust pursuant to Section&nbsp;2.03<A NAME="_Toc449767085"></A> hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;QIB Certificate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;As defined in Section&nbsp;5.5(a), a Rule 144A Agreement or a certificate substantially to the same<A NAME="_Toc449767086"></A> effect.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Qualification Defect&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to a Mortgage Loan, (a)&nbsp;a defective document in the Trustee Mortgage Loan File, (b)&nbsp;the absence of a document in the Trustee Mortgage Loan File, or (c)&nbsp;the breach of any representation, warranty or covenant with respect to the Mortgage Loan made by the applicable Seller or Servicer or the Depositor but only if the affected Mortgage Loan would cease to qualify as a &#147;qualified mortgage&#148; for purposes of the REMIC Provisions. &nbsp;With respect to a REMIC Regular Interest or a mortgage certificate described in Section&nbsp;860G(a)(3) of the Code, the failure to qualify as a &#147;qualified mortgage&#148; for purposes of the REMIC Pro<A NAME="_Toc449767087"></A>visions.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Qualified Institutional Buyer&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any &#147;qualified institutional buyer&#148; as defined in clause&nbsp;(a)(1) of Rule 144A.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767089"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Rating Agency&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any nationally recognized statistical rating agency, or its successor, that on the Closing Date rated one or more Classes of the Certificates at the request of the Depositor and identified in the Trust Agreement. &nbsp;If such agency or a successor is no longer in existence, the &#147;Rating Agency&#148; shall be such nationally recognized statistical rating agency, or other comparable Person, designated by the Depositor, notice of which designation shall be given to the Securities Administrator. &nbsp;References herein to any long-term rating category of a Rating Agency shall mean such rating category without regard to any plus or minus or numerical desi<A NAME="_Toc449767090"></A>gnation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Realized Loss<A NAME="_Toc449767091"></A>&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A Liquidation Loss, a Modification Loss or a Bankruptcy Loss, in each case, to the extent not covered by Insurance Proceeds.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Record Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Shall have the meaning set forth in the Trust Agreement<A NAME="_Toc449767092"></A>.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767096"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Regular Interest&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An interest in a REMIC that is designated in the Trust Agreement as a &#147;regular interest&#148; under the REMIC Pro<A NAME="_Toc449767097"></A>visions.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Regular Certificate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any Certificate other than a Residual Certificate and that represents a Regular Interest in a REMIC or a combination of Regular Interests in <A NAME="_Toc449767098"></A>a REMIC.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;REMIC&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to each Trust, each real estate mortgage investment conduit, within the meaning of the REMIC Provisions, for suc<A NAME="_Toc449767099"></A>h Trust.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;REMIC Provisions&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Provisions of the Code relating to real estate mortgage investment conduits, which appear at Sections&nbsp;860A through 860G of the Code, related Code provisions, and regulations, announcements and rulings thereunder, as the foregoing may be in effect from time <A NAME="_Toc449767100"></A>to time.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767101"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&nbsp;&#147;Remittance Report&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The report (either a data file or hard copy) that is prepared by each Servicer for the Master Servicer which contains the information specified in Schedule III hereto.<A NAME="_Toc449767102"></A></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;REO Disposition&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The receipt by the applicable Servicer of Insurance Proceeds and other payments and recoveries (including Liquidation Proceeds) which the Servicer recovers from the sale or other disposition of an REO P<A NAME="_Toc449767103"></A>roperty.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;REO Property&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Mortgaged Premises acquired by the Trust in foreclosure or similar actions.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Request for Release&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A request signed by an Officer of the Servicer, requesting that the Trustee (or applicable Custodian) release the Trustee Mortgage Loan File to such Servicer for the purpose set forth in such release, in accordance with the terms of the Servicing Agreement and these Standar<A NAME="_Toc449767104"></A>d Terms.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Reserve Fund&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Unless otherwise provided in the Trust Agreement, any fund in the Trust Estate other than (a)&nbsp;the Certificate Account, Distribution Account, the Master Servicer Account and Termination Account and (b)&nbsp;any other fund that is expressly excluded from <A NAME="_Toc449767105"></A>a REMIC.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Residual Certificate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Class R Certificates designated as such in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Residual Interest&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An interest in a REMIC that is designated as a &#147;residual interest&#148; under the REMIC Pro<A NAME="_Toc449767106"></A>visions.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767107"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Residual Transferee Agreement&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An agreement substantially in the form of <A NAME="_Toc449767108"></A><U>Exhibit&nbsp;F</U> hereto.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767111"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Responsible Officer&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;When used with respect to the Trustee or the Securities Administrator, any senior vice president, any vice president, any assistant vice president, any assistant treasurer, any trust officer, any assistant secretary in the Corporate Trust Office of the Trustee or the Securities Administrator, as the case may be, or any other officer of the Trustee or the Securities Administrator customarily performing functions similar to those performed by the persons who at the time shall be such officers and having direct responsibility for the administration of this Agreement, and also to whom with respect to a particular corporate trust matter such matter is referred because of such officer&#146;s knowledge of and familiarity with the particular subject; <I>provided, however</I>, when used with respect to the Master
 Servicer, any senior vice president, any assistant vice president, any trust officer, or any other officer of the Master Servicer customarily performing functions similar to those performed by any such named officer and having direct responsibility for the master servicing of the Mortgage Loans under this Trust Agreement. &nbsp;With respect to any other Person, the chairman of the board, the president, a vice president (however designated), the treasurer or controller.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Rule 144A&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Rule 144A promulgated by the Securities and Exchange Commission under the Securities Act, as the same may be amended from time <A NAME="_Toc449767109"></A>to time.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Rule 144A Agreement&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An agreement substantially in the form of <U>Exhibit&nbsp;C<A NAME="_Toc449767110"></A></U> hereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Rule 144A Certificates&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Any Class of Certificates designated as such in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Sale Agreement&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;<A NAME="_Toc449767112"></A>The Sale and Servicing Agreement or Sale and Servicing Agreements, as defined in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Scheduled Principal Balance&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;For any Mortgage Loan as of any Due Date subsequent to the Cut-Off Date up to and including the date on which such Mortgage Loan is finally liquidated or repurchased from the Trustee, the scheduled principal balance thereof as of the Cut-off Date, increased by the amount of negative amortization, if any, with respect thereto, and reduced by (i)&nbsp;the principal portion of all Monthly Payments due on or before such Due Date, whether or not paid by the Borrower or advanced by a Servicer, the Master Servicer, the Securities Administrator or an Insurer, net of any portion thereof that represents principal due on a Due Date occurring on or before the date on which such proceeds were received, (ii)&nbsp;the principal portion of all Prepayments, including Liquidation Proceeds, Condemnation Proceeds and Insurance Proceeds, and Pa
yoffs received on or before the last day of the Prepayment Period preceding such date of determination, and (iii)&nbsp;without duplication, the amount of any Realized Loss that has occurred with respect to such Mortgag<A NAME="_Toc449767113"></A>e Loan.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Securities Act&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Securities Act of 1933, as <A NAME="_Toc449767114"></A>amended.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Securities Administrator&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;As set forth in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Seller&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Loan Seller or Loan Sellers identified in the Trust Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767125"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Senior Collateral Group Percentage&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The percentage, if any, calculated as set forth in the Trust Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767126"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Senior Prepayment Percentage&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The percentage, if any, calculated as set forth in the Trust Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767127"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Series&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A group of Certificates issued by a separat<A NAME="_Toc449767128"></A>e Trust.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Servicemembers&#146; Shortfall&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Interest losses on a Mortgage Loan resulting from application of the Servicemembers&#146; Civil Relief Act, as amended.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Servicer&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Servicer or Servicers identified in the Servicing Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767129"></A>reement or Agreements.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767130"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Servicer Compensation&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Servicing Fee and any additional compensation as specified in the Servicing Agreement or Agr<A NAME="_Toc449767131"></A>eements.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Servicer Event of Default&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to each Servicer, shall have the meaning set forth in the applicable Servicing Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Servicer Mortgage Loan File&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to each Mortgage Loan, the related Mortgage File, as that term is defined in the related Servicing Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767132"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>&#147;<I>Servicer Remittance Date&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Shall mean the 18<SUP>th</SUP> day of each month or, if such day is not a Business Day, the next succeeding Business Day, or such other day as set forth in the related Sale and Servicing Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Servicing Agreement&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Sale and Servicing Agreement or Sale and Servicing Agreements, as defined in the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Servicing Fee&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Unless otherwise provided in the Trust Agreement, in any month, an amount equal to one-twelfth of the Servicing Fee Rate multiplied by the aggregate Scheduled Principal Balance of the Mortgage Loans as of the Due Date preceding a Distribution Date without taking into account any payment of principal due or made on such D<A NAME="_Toc449767133"></A>ue Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Servicing Fee Rate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The rate or rates specified as such in the applicable Servicing Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Shortfall&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Month End Interest Shortfall and Servicemembers&#146; Sh<A NAME="_Toc449767135"></A>ortfall.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767136"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&nbsp;&#147;Special Tax Consent&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The written consent of the Holder of a Residual Certificate to any tax (or risk thereof) arising out of a proposed transaction or activity that may be imposed upon such Holder or that may affect adversely the value of such Holder&#146;s Residual <A NAME="_Toc449767137"></A>Certificate.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Special Tax Opinion&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An Opinion of Counsel that a proposed transaction or activity will not (a)&nbsp;affect adversely the status of any REMIC as a REMIC or of the Regular Interests as the &#147;regular interests&#148; therein under the REMIC Provisions, (b)&nbsp;affect the payment of interest or principal on the Regular Interests, or (c)&nbsp;result in the encumbrance of the Mortgage Loans by a t<A NAME="_Toc449767138"></A>ax lien.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Standard Terms&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;These Standard Terms, as amended or supplemented, incorporated by reference in a Trust Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767139"></A>reement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767140"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Tax Matters Person&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The Securities Administrator which will act as tax matters person (within the meaning of the REMIC Provisions) of <A NAME="_Toc449767141"></A>a REMIC.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Terminating Purchase&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The purchase of all Mortgage Loans and each REO Property owned by a Trust pursuant to Section&nbsp;10.02<A NAME="_Toc449767142"></A> hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Termination Account&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An escrow account maintained by the Securities Administrator into which any Trust funds not distributed on the Distribution Date on which the earlier of (a)&nbsp;a Terminating Purchase or (b)&nbsp;the final payment or other Liquidation of the last Mortgage Loan remaining in the Trust or the disposition of the last REO Property remaining in the Trust is made are deposited. &nbsp;The Termination Account shall be an Eligible <A NAME="_Toc449767143"></A>Account.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Termination Price&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The sum of (i)&nbsp;an amount equal to 100% of the aggregate outstanding principal balance of each Mortgage Loan (other than Liquidated Mortgage Loans) remaining in the Trust on the day of such purchase, plus accrued interest thereon at the Note Rate and the amount of any outstanding Servicing Advances on such Mortgage Loans to the Due Date in the month in which the Termination Price is distributed to Certificateholders, less Bankruptcy Losses that would otherwise have been allocated to the Certificates and (ii) the lesser of (A) the Scheduled Principal Balance of the Mortgage Loan for any REO Property or other property remaining in the Trust, plus accrued interest thereon at the Note Rate (less the related Servicing Fee Rate) to the Due Date in the month in which the Termination Price is distributed to Certificateholders, and (B)&nb
sp;the sum of the aggregate fair market value of any such REO Property and all other property of the Trust, as determined by the Securities Administrator in consultation with the Initial Purchaser (or, if the Initial Purchaser is unwilling or unable to serve in that capacity, a financial advisor selected by the Securities Administrator in a commercially reasonable manner, whose fees will be an expense of the Depositor (or other party causing the Termination Purchase)), based upon the mean of bids from at least three recognized broker/dealers that deal in similar assets) as of the close of business on the third Business Day preceding the date upon which notice of any such termination is furnished to Certificateholders pursuant to Section&nbsp;9.03; <I>provided, however, </I>that in determining such aggregate fair market value, the Securities Administrator shall be entitled to conclusively rely on such bids or the opinion of a nationally recognized investment banker (the fees of which shall be an expense of th
e Trust). &nbsp;The fair market value of the REO Property and other property of the Trust shall be based upon the inclusion of (i) accrued interest to the last day of the month in which the Termination Price is distributed to the Certificateholders, at the applicable Note Rate (less the related Servicing Fee Rate) on the Scheduled Principal Balance of each Mortgage Loan related to an REO Property <A NAME="_Toc449767144"></A>and (ii) the amount of any costs and damages incurred by the Trust as a result of any violation of any applicable federal, state, or local predatory or abusive lending law arising from or in connection with the origination of any Mortgage Loans remaining in the Trust.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Transferee Agreement&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;An agreement substantially in the form of <A NAME="_Toc449767145"></A><U>Exhibit&nbsp;D</U> hereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trust&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The trust formed pursuant to the Trust<A NAME="_Toc449767146"></A> Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trust Agreement&#148;</I></B><I> or this</I><B><I> &#147;Agreement</I></B>: &nbsp;The Master Servicing and Trust Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, among the Depositor, Custodian, the Master Servicer, the Securities Administrator and the Trustee relating to the issuance of Certificates, and into which these Standard Terms are incorporated by re<A NAME="_Toc449767147"></A>ference.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trust Estate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The segregated pool of assets sold and assigned to the Trustee for the benefit of the Certificateholders by the Depositor pursuant to the conveyance clause&nbsp;of the Trust Ag<A NAME="_Toc449767148"></A>reement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trust Receipt&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;A certification as to the completeness of each Trustee Mortgage Loan File substantially in the form of <U>Exhibit&nbsp;A</U> hereto provided by the Securities Administrator (or the Custodian) pursuant to Section&nbsp;2.02<A NAME="_Toc449767149"></A> hereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trustee&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;The bank or trust company identified as the Trustee in the Trust Agreement, and its successors and <A NAME="_Toc449767150"></A>assigns.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trustee Advance&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Not applicable.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767151"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trustee Fee&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;<A NAME="_Toc449767152"></A>Not applicable.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trustee Fee Rate&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;Not applicable.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc449767153"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B><I>&#147;Trustee Mortgage Loan File&#148;</I></B>: &nbsp;With respect to each Mortgage Loan, unless otherwise provided in the Trust Agreement, collectively, the following documents, together with any other Mortgage Loan documents held by the Trustee or the related Custodian with respect to such Mortgage Loan:</P>
