<P style="page-break-before:always; margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=right><B>Exhibit&nbsp;F</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>FORM OF RESIDUAL TRANSFEREE AGREEMENT</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:252pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">_________________</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:252pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(DATE)</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">GS Mortgage Securities Corp.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">85 Broad Street</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">New York, New York 10004</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Wachovia Bank, National Association,</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;as Trustee</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">401 South Tryon Street, 12<SUP>th</SUP> Floor</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Charlotte, NC 28288-1179</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Attention: &nbsp;Corporate Trust Services</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Re:</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Master Servicing and Trust Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, among GS Mortgage Securities Corp., as Depositor, Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, as Master Servicer, JPMorgan Chase Bank, National Association, as Securities Administrator, and Wachovia Bank, National Association, as Trustee of GSR Mortgage Loan Trust&nbsp;2004-15F</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Ladies and Gentlemen:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">In connection with the purchase on the date hereof of the captioned securities (the &#147;Residual Certificate&#148;), to be issued pursuant to the Master Servicing and Trust Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, among GS Mortgage Securities Corp., Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, as Master Servicer, JPMorgan Chase Bank, National Association, as Securities Administrator, and Wachovia Bank, National Association, as Trustee (the &#147;Trustee&#148;) which incorporates by reference the Standard Terms to Trust Agreement, November 2004 Edition (the &#147;Standard Terms to Trust Agreement&#148;) (collectively, the &#147;Trust Agreement&#148;), the undersigned hereby certifies and covenants to the transferor, the Depositor, the Trustee and the Trust as follows:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">1.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We certify that on the date hereof we have simultaneously herewith delivered to you an affidavit certifying, among other things, that (A)&nbsp;we are not a Disqualified Organization and (B)&nbsp;we are not purchasing such Residual Certificate on behalf of a Disqualified Organization. &nbsp;We understand that any breach by us of this certification may cause us to be liable for a tax imposed upon transfers to Disqualified Organizations.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">2.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We acknowledge that we will be the beneficial owner of the Residual Certificate and that the Residual Certificate will be registered in our name and not in the name of a nominee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">3.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We certify that no purpose of our purchase of the Residual Certificate is to avoid or impede the assessment or collection of tax.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">4.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(A)&nbsp;We understand that the Residual Certificate represents for federal income tax purposes a &#147;residual interest&#148; in a real estate mortgage investment conduit and (B)&nbsp;we understand that as the holder of the Residual Certificate we will be required to take into account, in determining our taxable income, our pro rata percentage interest of the taxable income of each REMIC formed pursuant to the Trust Agreement in accordance with all applicable provisions of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">5.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We understand that if, notwithstanding the transfer restrictions, any of the Residual Certificates is in fact transferred to a Disqualified Organization, a tax may be imposed on the transferor of such Residual Certificate. &nbsp;We agree that any breach by us of these representations shall render such transfer of such Residual Certificate by us absolutely null and void and shall cause no rights in the Residual Certificate to vest in the transferee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">6.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The sale to us and our purchase of the Residual Certificates constitutes a sale for tax and all other purposes and each party thereto has received due and adequate consideration. &nbsp;In our view, the transaction represents fair value, representing the results of arms length negotiations and taking into account our analysis of the tax and other consequences of investment in the Residual Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">7.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Unless this provision is explicitly waived by the transferor to us of the Residual Certificates, we expect that the purchase of the Residual Certificates, together with the receipt of the price, if any, therefor will be economically neutral or profitable to us overall, after all related expenses (including taxes) have been paid and based on conservative assumptions with respect to discount rates, prepayments and other factors necessary to evaluate profitability.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">8.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We are a &#147;U.S. Person&#148; within the meaning of Section&nbsp;7701(a)(30) of the Code. &nbsp;We are duly organized and validly existing under the laws of the jurisdiction of our organization. &nbsp;We are neither bankrupt nor insolvent nor do we have reason to believe that we will become bankrupt or insolvent. &nbsp;We have conducted and are conducting our business so as to comply in all material respects with all applicable statutes and regulations. &nbsp;The person executing and delivering this letter on our behalf is duly authorized to do so, the execution and delivery by us of this letter and the consummation of the transaction on the terms set forth herein are within our corporate power, and upon such execution and delivery, this letter will constitute our legal, valid and binding obligation, enforceable against us in accordance with its terms, subject, as to the enforceme
nt of remedies, to applicable bankruptcy, reorganization, insolvency, moratorium and other laws affecting the right of creditors generally and to general principles of equity and the discretion of the court (regardless of whether enforcement of such remedies is considered in a proceeding in equity or at law).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">9.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Neither the execution and delivery by us of this letter, nor the compliance by us with the provisions hereof, nor the consummation by us of the transactions as set forth herein, will (A)&nbsp;conflict with or result in a breach of, or constitute a default or result in the acceleration of any obligation under, our certificate of incorporation or by-laws or, after giving effect to the consents or the taking of the actions contemplated by clause&nbsp;(B)&nbsp;of this subparagraph, any of the provisions of any law, governmental rule, regulation, judgment, decree or order binding on us or our properties, or any of the provisions of any indenture or mortgage or any other contract or instrument to which we are a party or by which we or any of our properties is bound, or (B)&nbsp;require the consent of or notice to or any filing with, any person, entity or governmental body, which has not be
en obtained or made by us.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">10.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We anticipate being a profit-making entity on an ongoing basis.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">11.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We have filed all required federal and state income tax returns and have paid all federal and state income taxes due; we intend to file and pay all such returns and taxes in the future. &nbsp;We acknowledge that as the holder of the Residual Certificates, to the extent the Residual Certificates would be treated as a noneconomic residual interest within the meaning of U.S. Treasury Regulation Section&nbsp;1.860E-1(c)(2), we may incur tax liabilities in excess of cash flows generated by the Residual Certificates and that we intend to pay taxes associated with holding the Residual Certificates as they become due.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">12.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We agree that in the event that at some future time we wish to transfer any interest in the Residual Certificates, we will transfer such interest in the Residual Certificates only to a transferee that:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(a)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">is not a Disqualified Organization and is not purchasing such interest in the Residual Certificates on behalf of a Disqualified Organization, and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">(b)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">has delivered to the Trustee a transferee agreement in the form of Exhibit&nbsp;D to the Standard Terms to Trust Agreement and an affidavit in the form of Exhibit&nbsp;G-1 or Exhibit&nbsp;G-2, as applicable, to the Standard Terms to Trust Agreement and, if requested by the Trustee, an opinion of counsel, in form acceptable to the Trustee, that the proposed transfer will not cause the Residual Certificates to be held by a Disqualified Organization.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">13.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We are knowledgeable and experienced in financial, business and tax matters generally and in particular, the investment risks and tax consequences of REMIC residuals that provide little or no cash flow, and are capable of evaluating the merits and risks of an investment in the Residual Certificates; we are able to bear the economic risks of an investment in the Residual Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">14.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">In addition, we acknowledge that the Trustee will not register the transfer of a Residual Certificate to a transferee that is not a &#147;U.S. Person&#148; within the meaning of Section&nbsp;7701(a)(30) of the Code. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">15.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Capitalized terms used herein but not defined herein shall have the meanings ascribed to such terms in the Standard Terms to Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">16.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">We hereby designate the Trustee as our fiduciary to perform the duties of the tax matters person for each REMIC formed pursuant to the Trust Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center>(signature page follows)</P>

<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>FORM OF NON-U.S. PERSON AFFIDAVIT</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>AND AFFIDAVIT PURSUANT TO SECTIONS</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>860D(a)(6)(A) and 860E(e)(4)</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>OF THE INTERNAL REVENUE CODE OF 1986, AS AMENDED</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Re:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>GS Mortgage Securities Corp., Depositor</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>GSR Mortgage Loan Trust</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>2004-15F &nbsp;(the &#147;Trust&#148;)</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">STATE OF ____________________</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:180pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">)</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:180pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">)</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:216pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">ss.:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">CITY OF ______________________</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:216pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">)</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Under penalties of perjury, I, the undersigned, declare that to the best of my knowledge and belief, the following representations are true, correct and complete:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">1.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">I am a duly authorized officer of ___________________ (the &#147;Transferee&#148;), and on behalf of which I have the authority to make this affidavit.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">2.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee is acquiring all or a portion of the securities (the &#147;Residual Certificates&#148;), which represent a residual interest in one or more real estate mortgage investment conduits (each, a &#147;REMIC&#148;) for which elections are to be made under Section&nbsp;860D of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">3.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee is a foreign person within the meaning of Treasury Regulation Section&nbsp;1.860G-3(a)(1) (<I>i.e.</I>, a person other than (i)&nbsp;a citizen or resident of the United States, (ii)&nbsp;a corporation or partnership that is organized under the laws of the United States or any jurisdiction thereof or therein, (iii)&nbsp;an estate that is subject to United States federal income tax regardless of the source of its income or (iv)&nbsp;a trust if a court within the United States is able to exercise primary supervision over the administration of such trust and one or more United States Persons have the authority to control all substantial decisions of the trust) who would be subject to United States income tax withholding pursuant to Section&nbsp;1441 or 1442 of the Code on income derived from the Residual Certificates (a &#147;Non-U.S. Person&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">4.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee agrees that it will not hold the Residual Certificates in connection with a trade or business in the United States, and the Transferee understands that it will be subject to United States federal income tax under Sections&nbsp;871 and 881 of the Code in accordance with Section&nbsp;860G of the Code and any Treasury regulations issued thereunder on &#147;excess inclusions&#148; that accrue with respect to the Residual Certificates during the period the Transferee holds the Residual Certificates.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">5.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee understands that the federal income tax on excess inclusions with respect to the Residual Certificates may be withheld in accordance with Section&nbsp;860G(b) of the Code from distributions that otherwise would be made to the Transferee on the Residual Certificates and, to the extent that such tax has not been imposed previously, that such tax may be imposed at the time of disposition of any such Residual Certificate pursuant to Section&nbsp;860G(b) of the Code.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">6.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee agrees (i)&nbsp;to file a timely United States federal income tax return for the year in which disposition of a Residual Certificate it holds occurs (or earlier if required by law) and will pay any United States federal income tax due at that time and (ii)&nbsp;if any tax is due at that time, to provide satisfactory written evidence of payment of such tax to the Trustee or its designated paying agent or other person who is liable to withhold federal income tax from a distribution on the Residual Certificates under Sections&nbsp;1441 and 1442 of the Code and the regulations thereunder (the &#147;Withholding Agent&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">7.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee understands that until it provides written evidence of the payment of tax due upon the disposition of a Residual Certificate to the Withholding Agent pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;6 above, the Withholding Agent may (i)&nbsp;withhold an amount equal to such tax from future distributions made with respect to the Residual Certificate to subsequent transferees (after giving effect to the withholding of taxes imposed on such subsequent transferees), and (ii)&nbsp;pay the withheld amount to the Internal Revenue Service.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">8.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee understands that (i)&nbsp;the Withholding Agent may withhold other amounts required to be withheld pursuant to United States federal income tax law, if any, from distributions that otherwise would be made to such transferee on each Residual Certificate it holds and (ii)&nbsp;the Withholding Agent may pay to the Internal Revenue Service amounts withheld on behalf of any and all former holders of each Residual Certificate held by the Transferee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">9.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee understands that if it transfers a Residual Certificate (or any interest therein) to a United States Person (including a foreign person who is subject to net United States federal income taxation with respect to such Residual Certificate), the Withholding Agent may disregard the transfer for federal income tax purposes if the transfer would have the effect of allowing the Transferee to avoid tax on accrued excess inclusions and may continue to withhold tax from future distributions as though the Residual Certificate were still held by the Transferee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">10.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee understands that a transfer of a Residual Certificate (or any interest therein) to a Non-U.S. Person (<I>i.e.</I>, a foreign person who is not subject to net United States federal income tax with respect to such Residual Certificate) will not be recognized unless the Withholding Agent has received from the transferee an affidavit in substantially the same form as this affidavit containing these same agreements and representations.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">11.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee understands that distributions on a Residual Certificate may be delayed, without interest, pending determination of amounts to be withheld.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">12.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee is not a &#147;Disqualified Organization&#148; (as defined below), and the Transferee is not acquiring a Residual Certificate for the account of, or as agent or nominee of, or with a view to the transfer of direct or indirect record or beneficial ownership to, a Disqualified Organization. &nbsp;For the purposes hereof, a Disqualified Organization is any of the following: &nbsp;(i)&nbsp;the United States, any State or political subdivision thereof, any foreign government, any international organization, or any agency or instrumentality of any of the foregoing; (ii)&nbsp;any organization (other than a farmer&#146;s cooperative as defined in Section&nbsp;521 of the Code) that is exempt from federal income taxation (including taxation under the unrelated business taxable income provisions of the Code); (iii)&nbsp;any rural telephone or electrical service cooperative descri
bed in Section&nbsp;1381(a)(2)(C) of the Code; or (iv)&nbsp;any other entity treated as a &#147;disqualified organization&#148; within the meaning of Section&nbsp;860E(e)(5) of the Code. &nbsp;In addition, a corporation will not be treated as an instrumentality of the United States or of any state or political subdivision thereof if all of its activities are subject to tax and, with the exception of the Federal Home Loan Mortgage Corporation, a majority of its board of directors is not selected by such governmental unit.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">13.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee agrees to consent to any amendment of the Trust Agreement that shall be deemed necessary by the Depositor (upon the advice of counsel to the Depositor) to constitute a reasonable arrangement to ensure that no interest in a Residual Certificate will be owned directly or indirectly by a Disqualified Organization.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">14.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee acknowledges that Section&nbsp;860E(e) of the Code would impose a substantial tax on the transferor or, in certain circumstances, on an agent for the Transferee, with respect to any transfer of any interest in any Residual Certificate to a Disqualified Organization.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Capitalized terms used and not otherwise defined herein shall have the meanings assigned to them in the Master Servicing and Trust Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, which incorporates by reference the Standard Terms thereto, among GS Mortgage Securities Corp., Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, JPMorgan Chase Bank, National Association and the Trustee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the Transferee has caused this instrument to be duly executed on its behalf, by its duly authorized officer as of the _______ day of _____________, 20__.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:216pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><U>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</U></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:216pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>[Name of Transferee]</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:216pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>By:<U> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</U></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:216pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Its:<U> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</U></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Personally appeared before me ___________________________, known or proved to me to be the same person who executed the foregoing instrument and to be a ______________________ of the Transferee, and acknowledged to me that he or she executed the same as his or her free act and deed and as the free act and deed of the Transferee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Subscribed and sworn before me this ______ day of __________, 20__.</P>

<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>860D(a)(6)(A) and 860E(e)(4)</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>OF THE INTERNAL REVENUE CODE OF 1986, AS AMENDED</B></P>

<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Under penalties of perjury, I, the undersigned declare that, to the best of my knowledge and belief, the following representations are true, correct and complete:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">1.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">I am a duly authorized officer of ______________________ (the &#147;Transferee&#148;), on behalf of which I have the authority to make this affidavit.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">2.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee is acquiring all or a portion of the securities (the &#147;Residual Certificates&#148;), which represent a residual interest in one or more real estate mortgage investment conduits (each, a &#147;REMIC&#148;) for which elections are to be made under Section&nbsp;860D of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">3.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee either is (i)&nbsp;a citizen or resident of the United States, (ii)&nbsp;a domestic partnership or corporation, (iii)&nbsp;an estate that is subject to United States federal income tax regardless of the source of its income, (iv)&nbsp;a trust if a court within the United States is able to exercise primary supervision over the administration of such trust and one or more United States Persons have the authority to control all substantial decisions of the trust, or (v)&nbsp;a foreign person who would be subject to United States income taxation on a net basis on income derived from the Residual Certificates (a &#147;U.S. Person&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">4.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee is a not a &#147;Disqualified Organization&#148; (as defined below), and the Transferee is not acquiring a Residual Certificate for the account of, or as agent or nominee of, or with a view to the transfer of direct or indirect record or beneficial ownership to, a Disqualified Organization. &nbsp;For the purposes hereof, a Disqualified Organization is any of the following: &nbsp;(i)&nbsp;the United States, any state or political subdivision thereof, any foreign government, any international organization, or any agency or instrumentality of any of the foregoing; (ii)&nbsp;any organization (other than a farmer&#146;s cooperative as defined in Section&nbsp;521 of the Code) that is exempt from federal income taxation (including taxation under the unrelated business taxable income provisions of the Code); (iii)&nbsp;any rural telephone or electrical service cooperative desc
ribed in &#167;&nbsp;1381(a)(2)(C) of the Code; or (iv)&nbsp;any other entity treated as a &#147;disqualified organization&#148; within the meaning of Section&nbsp;860E(e)(5) of the Code. &nbsp;In addition, a corporation will not be treated as an instrumentality of the United States or of any state or political subdivision thereof if all of its activities are subject to tax and, with the exception of the Federal Home Loan Mortgage Corporation, a majority of its board of directors is not selected by such governmental unit.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">5.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee agrees to consent to any amendment of the Trust Agreement that shall be deemed necessary by the Depositor (upon the advice of counsel to the Depositor) to constitute a reasonable arrangement to ensure that no interest in a Residual Certificate will be owned directly or indirectly by a Disqualified Organization.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">6.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The Transferee acknowledges that Section&nbsp;860E(e) of the Code would impose a substantial tax on the transferor or, in certain circumstances, on an agent for the Transferee, with respect to any transfer of any interest in any Residual Certificate to a Disqualified Organization.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Capitalized terms used and not otherwise defined herein shall have the meanings assigned to them in the Master Servicing and Trust Agreement, dated as of November 1, 2004, which incorporates by reference the Standard Terms thereto, among GS Mortgage Securities Corp., Chase Manhattan Mortgage Corporation, JPMorgan Chase Bank, National Association and the Trustee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the Transferee has caused this instrument to be duly executed on its behalf, by its duly authorized officer this ____ day of ______, 20__.</P>

</TD><TD style="border-right:0.5pt solid #000000; border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000" valign=top width=44.4><P style="margin:0pt; line-height:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6pt">Servicer Loan Number - loan number used at your company.</P>
</TD><TD style="border-right:0.5pt solid #000000; border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000" valign=top width=38.867><P style="margin:0pt; line-height:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6pt">Loan number used by Investor</P>

</TD><TD style="border-right:0.5pt solid #000000; border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000" valign=top width=44.133><P style="margin:0pt; line-height:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6pt">Net interest paid the loan was paid-in-full</P>
</TD><TD style="border-right:0.5pt solid #000000; border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000" valign=top width=46><P style="margin:0pt; line-height:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6pt">Enter the date the loan was paid-in-full. Leave blank if no PIF transaction.</P>
</TD><TD style="border-right:0.5pt solid #000000; border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000" valign=top width=59.8><P style="margin:0pt; line-height:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6pt">Beginning scheduled note rate before the servicer's monthly activity. &nbsp;Can be blank for act/act pools.</P>
</TD><TD style="border-right:0.5pt solid #000000; border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000" valign=top width=76.333><P style="margin:0pt; line-height:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6pt">Ending scheduled loan note rate after servicer's monthly activity (sch/sch) or the ending actual loan note rate after servicer's activity (act/act).</P>
</TD><TD style="border-right:0.5pt solid #000000; border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000" valign=top width=68.733><P style="margin:0pt; line-height:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6pt">Beginning scheduled servicer service fee rate before the servicer's monthly activity. &nbsp;Can be blank for act/act pools.</P>
</TD><TD style="border-right:0.5pt solid #000000; border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000" valign=top width=65.533><P style="margin:0pt; line-height:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6pt">Ending scheduled servicer service fee rate after the servicer's monthly activity.</P>

<BR>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>GS MORTGAGE SECURITIES CORP., DEPOSITOR<BR>
MORTGAGE PASS-THROUGH CERTIFICATES, SERIES 2004-15F<BR>
CLASS [ &nbsp;&nbsp;] CERTIFICATE</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>UNLESS THIS CERTIFICATE IS PRESENTED BY AN AUTHORIZED REPRESENTATIVE OF THE DEPOSITORY TRUST COMPANY, A NEW YORK CORPORATION (&#147;DTC&#148;), TO THE TRUSTEE, IN ITS CAPACITY AS CUSTODIAN FOR DTC (IN SUCH CAPACITY, THE &#147;CUSTODIAN&#148;) OR ITS AGENT FOR REGISTRATION OF TRANSFER, EXCHANGE, OR PAYMENT, AND ANY CERTIFICATE ISSUED IS REGISTERED IN THE NAME OF CEDE &amp; CO. OR IN SUCH OTHER NAME AS IS REQUESTED BY AN AUTHORIZED REPRESENTATIVE OF DTC (AND ANY PAYMENT MADE TO CEDE &amp; CO. OR TO SUCH OTHER ENTITY AS IS REQUESTED BY AN AUTHORIZED REPRESENTATIVE OF DTC), ANY TRANSFER, PLEDGE, OR OTHER USE HEREOF FOR VALUE OR OTHERWISE BY OR TO ANY PERSON IS WRONGFUL INASMUCH AS THE REGISTERED OWNER HEREOF, CEDE &amp; CO., HAS AN INTEREST HEREIN.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>[THE YIELD TO THE HOLDER OF THIS CERTIFICATE WILL BE EXTREMELY SENSITIVE TO THE RATE OF PRINCIPAL PAYMENTS (INCLUDING PREPAYMENTS) ON THE MORTGAGE LOANS.]</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>[THIS CLASS [ &nbsp;&nbsp;] CERTIFICATE SHALL NOT BE ENTITLED TO ANY DISTRIBUTIONS WITH RESPECT TO PRINCIPAL.]</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>[THIS CLASS [ &nbsp;&nbsp;] CERTIFICATE IS SUBORDINATED TO THE EXTENT DESCRIBED HEREIN AND IN THE TRUST AGREEMENT REFERENCED HEREIN.]</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>THIS CLASS [ &nbsp;&nbsp;] CERTIFICATE REPRESENTS A REMIC REGULAR INTEREST FOR FEDERAL INCOME TAX PURPOSES.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>THE PRINCIPAL OF THIS CLASS [ &nbsp;&nbsp;] CERTIFICATE IS SUBJECT TO PREPAYMENT FROM TIME TO TIME WITHOUT SURRENDER OF OR NOTATION ON THIS CERTIFICATE. ACCORDINGLY, THE CERTIFICATE PRINCIPAL BALANCE OF THIS CERTIFICATE MAY BE LESS THAN THAT SET FORTH BELOW. ANYONE ACQUIRING THIS CERTIFICATE MAY ASCERTAIN ITS CURRENT CERTIFICATE PRINCIPAL BALANCE BY INQUIRY OF THE CUSTODIAN.</B></P>
<BR>

<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>

<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:36pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">evidencing a beneficial ownership interest in a Trust Fund consisting of the entire beneficial ownership of a pool of certain fixed-rate, one- to four-family, first lien Mortgage Loans formed and sold by</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>

ficate is issued under and is subject to the terms, provisions and conditions of the Trust Agreement and also is subject to certain terms and conditions set forth in (i) the Assignment, Assumption and Recognition Agreement by and among GSMC, the Depositor and ABN AMRO Mortgage Group, Inc.
